


atmosphere: ▶The atmosphere at the dinner party was warm and friendly. (晚宴上的气氛温暖而友好。) ▶They are studying the chemical composition of Jupiter's atmosphere. (他们正在研究木星大气的化学成分。)
hydrosphere: ▶The hydrosphere includes all the water on Earth's surface, such as oceans, lakes, and rivers. (水圈包括地球表面所有的水，例如海洋、湖泊和河流。)
lithosphere: ▶The lithosphere is the rigid outer layer of the Earth, consisting of the crust and upper mantle. (岩石圈是地球的刚性外层，包括地壳和上地幔。)
oxygen: ▶We need to breathe oxygen to live. (我们需要呼吸氧气才能生存。) ▶The diver checked his oxygen tank before going underwater. (潜水员在下水前检查了他的氧气罐。)
oxide: ▶Rust is a form of iron oxide. (锈是一种氧化铁。) ▶Carbon monoxide is a poisonous gas, while carbon dioxide is a common oxide. (一氧化碳是有毒气体，而二氧化碳是一种常见的氧化物。)
carbon dioxide: ▶Plants absorb carbon dioxide and release oxygen. (植物吸收二氧化碳并释放氧气。)
hydrogen: ▶Hydrogen is the lightest element in the universe. (氢是宇宙中最轻的元素。) ▶A hydrogen bomb is an extremely powerful weapon. (氢弹是一种威力极大的武器。)
core: ▶The Earth's core is believed to be composed primarily of iron and nickel. (地核被认为主要由铁和镍构成。) ▶This argument gets to the core of the issue. (这个论点触及了问题的核心。) ▶I need to do some exercises to strengthen my core muscles. (我需要做一些运动来增强我的核心肌肉。)
crust: ▶The Earth's crust is thinner under the oceans. (在海洋下方，地壳更薄。) ▶She cut the crusts off her sandwich. (她切掉了三明治的面包皮。)
mantle: ▶The Earth's mantle lies between the crust and the core. (地幔位于地壳和地核之间。) ▶He is expected to take up the mantle of leadership after his father retires. (预计他将在父亲退休后接过领导重任。)
longitude: ▶The longitude of Beijing is about 116 degrees east. (北京的经度大约是东经116度。)
latitude: ▶The island is located at a latitude of 40 degrees north. (该岛位于北纬40度。) ▶The new policy allows teachers considerable latitude in choosing teaching materials. (新政策给予教师在选择教材上相当大的自由。)
horizon: ▶The sun dipped below the horizon. (太阳落到了地平线以下。) ▶This new discovery opens up new horizons in medical research. (这一新发现开启了医学研究的新视野。)
altitude: ▶The plane is now flying at an altitude of 10,000 meters. (飞机现在在海拔一万米的高度飞行。)
disaster: ▶The earthquake was a terrible disaster. (那场地震是一场可怕的灾难。) ▶The party was a complete disaster; almost no one showed up. (那个派对彻底搞砸了，几乎没人来。)
mishap: ▶The journey went smoothly, without any mishaps. (旅途顺利，没有任何意外。)
catastrophic: ▶The catastrophic floods destroyed thousands of homes. (灾难性的洪水摧毁了数千所房屋。)
calamity: ▶The eruption of the volcano was a terrible calamity for the islanders. (火山爆发对岛民来说是一场可怕的灾难。)
endanger: ▶Pollution can endanger many species of wildlife. (污染会危及许多野生动植物物种。)
jeopardise: ▶Revealing the secret would jeopardise the entire mission. (泄露秘密会危及整个任务。)
destructive: ▶The hurricane was incredibly destructive. (那次飓风具有惊人的破坏力。) ▶He has a destructive habit of criticising everyone. (他有一个批评所有人的破坏性习惯。)
El Nino: ▶El Nino events can cause severe droughts in some regions and heavy rains in others. (厄尔尼诺现象会导致一些地区严重干旱，而另一些地区暴雨成灾。)
greenhouse: ▶We grow tomatoes in the greenhouse. (我们在温室里种西红柿。) ▶Carbon dioxide is a major greenhouse gas. (二氧化碳是一种主要的温室气体。)
phenomenon: ▶The northern lights are a beautiful natural phenomenon. (北极光是一种美丽的自然现象。) ▶He is a phenomenon on the basketball court. (他是篮球场上的一个奇才。)
pebble: ▶She skipped a pebble across the surface of the lake. (她让一块鹅卵石掠过湖面。)
magnet: ▶This metal is not a magnet, but it can be magnetised. (这种金属不是磁铁，但可以被磁化。) ▶The new art gallery has become a magnet for tourists. (新美术馆已成为吸引游客的地方。)
ore: ▶The company mines iron ore in this region. (该公司在这个地区开采铁矿石。)
mineral: ▶The body requires essential minerals like calcium and iron to function properly. (人体需要钙和铁等必需矿物质才能正常运作。) ▶Mineral water is bottled directly from the spring. (矿泉水是从泉源直接装瓶的。)
marble: ▶The statue was carved from a single block of white marble. (这座雕像是由一整块白色大理石雕刻而成的。) ▶The floor of the grand hall was made of polished marble. (大厅的地板是由抛光过的大理石制成的。) ▶Let's have a game of marbles. (我们玩打弹子游戏吧。)
quartz: ▶This watch contains a quartz crystal for accurate timekeeping. (这块手表装有石英晶体以确保计时准确。)
granite: ▶The kitchen countertops are made of durable granite. (厨房的操作台是由耐用的花岗岩制成的。)
gust: ▶A sudden gust of wind blew his hat off. (一阵突然的狂风把他的帽子吹掉了。)
breeze: ▶A gentle breeze rustled the leaves. (微风拂过，树叶沙沙作响。) ▶The exam was a breeze for her. (那次考试对她来说易如反掌。)
monsoon: ▶The monsoon season brings heavy rains to Southeast Asia. (季风季节给东南亚带来强降雨。)
gale: ▶The ship was delayed due to gale-force winds. (由于遭遇大风，船延误了。)
hurricane: ▶The hurricane caused widespread damage along the coast. (飓风给沿海地区造成了大规模的破坏。)
tornado: ▶A tornado touched down, destroying several homes. (一股龙卷风着陆，摧毁了几栋房屋。)
typhoon: ▶The typhoon is expected to make landfall tomorrow. (预计台风将于明天登陆。)
volcano: ▶Mount Fuji is an active volcano in Japan. (富士山是日本的一座活火山。)
erupt: ▶The volcano could erupt at any time. (这座火山随时可能喷发。) ▶Violence erupted in the streets after the announcement. (消息宣布后，街头爆发了暴力事件。) ▶He erupted into laughter. (他突然大笑起来。)
magma: ▶Magma is molten rock beneath the Earth's surface. (岩浆是地表以下的熔融岩石。)
thermodynamic: ▶The engineer specialized in thermodynamic systems. (这位工程师专攻热力学系统。)
smog: ▶The city was covered in a thick layer of smog. (城市被厚厚的烟雾笼罩着。)
fume: ▶She could smell the fumes from the exhaust pipe. (她能闻到排气管排出的烟气。) ▶He was fuming with rage after the argument. (争吵过后，他怒火中烧。)
mist: ▶The hills were shrouded in a light morning mist. (山丘笼罩在晨雾中。) ▶She misted the plants with a spray bottle. (她用喷雾瓶给植物喷了水。)
tsunami: ▶The earthquake triggered a devastating tsunami. (地震引发了破坏性的海啸。)
drought: ▶The region has suffered from a severe drought for three years. (该地区已遭受严重干旱三年之久。)
flooding: ▶The heavy rain caused severe flooding in the city. (大雨在城市中造成了严重的内涝。)
torrent: ▶The rain fell in torrents. (大雨倾盆而下。) ▶He received a torrent of abuse from the crowd. (他遭到了人群的谩骂攻击。)
earthquake: ▶The earthquake measured 7.0 on the Richter scale. (这次地震的震级为里氏7.0级。)
seismic: ▶The country is conducting a seismic survey to locate oil reserves. (该国正在进行地震勘探以定位石油储量。) ▶This decision will have a seismic impact on the industry. (这一决定将对行业产生巨大的影响。)
avalanche: ▶Skiers were warned of the high risk of avalanche. (滑雪者被警告有很高的雪崩风险。) ▶The press secretary faced an avalanche of questions. (新闻秘书面临一连串的问题。)
terrain: ▶The rugged terrain made the journey difficult. (崎岖的地形使旅途变得艰难。)
landscape: ▶The landscape of the desert is breathtaking. (沙漠的景色令人叹为观止。) ▶The political landscape has changed dramatically. (政治格局已发生巨变。)
continent: ▶Asia is the largest continent on Earth. (亚洲是地球上最大的大陆。)
cave: ▶The explorers discovered ancient paintings in the cave. (探险家在洞穴里发现了古老的壁画。)
cliff: ▶The castle was built on top of a high cliff. (城堡建在高高的悬崖顶上。)
glacier: ▶The glacier has been retreating rapidly due to global warming. (由于全球变暖，冰川一直在迅速消退。)
swamp: ▶The boots are designed for walking through swampy terrain. (这靴子是为穿越沼泽地设计的。) ▶I've been swamped with work this week. (这周我工作忙得不可开交。)
delta: ▶The Nile Delta is a very fertile region. (尼罗河三角洲是一个非常肥沃的地区。)
plain: ▶Vast plains stretched out before them. (广阔的平原在他们面前延伸开来。) ▶Her meaning was quite plain to everyone. (她的意思大家都明白。) ▶She was dressed in a plain black dress. (她穿着一件朴素的黑色连衣裙。)
plateau: ▶The ranch is on a large plateau surrounded by mountains. (牧场位于一个被山脉环绕的大高原上。) ▶After a period of rapid growth, sales have now plateaued. (经过一段时间的快速增长后，销售额现已趋于平稳。)
oasis: ▶The travelers found an oasis in the desert. (旅行者在沙漠中发现了一片绿洲。) ▶The city park is a welcome oasis of calm. (城市公园是一个受人欢迎的宁静绿洲。)
globe: ▶They have business interests across the globe. (他们在全球都有商业利益。) ▶She spun the globe and pointed to a random country. (她转动地球仪，随机指向一个国家。)
hemisphere: ▶The Northern Hemisphere experiences summer when the Southern Hemisphere experiences winter. (北半球是夏天时，南半球是冬天。)
equator: ▶Singapore is located very close to the equator. (新加坡位于非常靠近赤道的地方。)
arctic: ▶The Arctic ice is melting at an alarming rate. (北极冰层正以惊人的速度融化。) ▶The weather was arctic this morning. (今天早上天气极冷。)
Antarctic: ▶Penguins are native to the Antarctic region. (企鹅原产于南极地区。)
pole: ▶The Earth's geographic North Pole is located in the Arctic. (地球的地理北极位于北极地区。) ▶The tent was supported by wooden poles. (帐篷用木杆支撑着。)
polar: ▶Polar bears are well adapted to the cold environment. (北极熊非常适应寒冷的环境。) ▶The two politicians hold polar opinions on this issue. (这两位政治家在这个问题上持有截然相反的意见。)
axis: ▶The Earth rotates on its axis once every 24 hours. (地球每24小时绕地轴自转一周。) ▶The alliance formed a new political axis. (该联盟形成了一个新的政治轴心。)
deteriorate: ▶The political situation in the region began to deteriorate rapidly. (该地区的政治局势开始迅速恶化。) ▶His health deteriorated after the operation. (手术后他的健康状况恶化了。)
aggravate: ▶His comments only served to aggravate the situation. (他的评论只会使情况恶化。) ▶The noise aggravates my headache. (噪音加剧了我的头痛。)
degrade: ▶Plastic bags can take hundreds of years to degrade. (塑料袋可能需要数百年才能降解。) ▶No one should be degraded because of their race or gender. (任何人都不应因其种族或性别而受辱。)
upgrade: ▶We upgraded our seats to business class. (我们将座位升级到了商务舱。) ▶The company is upgrading its computer systems. (公司正在升级其计算机系统。)
erode: ▶Coastlines are eroded by the sea over time. (海岸线随着时间的推移受到海水的侵蚀。) ▶Public confidence in the government has been eroded. (公众对政府的信心已被削弱。)
Mediterranean: ▶They spent their holiday on a Mediterranean cruise. (他们在一次地中海巡航中度过了假期。)
Atlantic: ▶The Atlantic Ocean separates Europe and Africa from the Americas. (大西洋将欧洲和非洲与美洲隔开。)
pacific: ▶The Pacific Ocean is the largest ocean on Earth. (太平洋是地球上最大的海洋。) ▶He spoke in a pacific tone, trying to calm everyone down. (他以一种平和的语气说话，试图让每个人都冷静下来。)
ocean: ▶The ship sailed across the vast ocean. (船航行在广阔的海洋上。)
marine: ▶The area is rich in marine life. (该地区海洋生物丰富。) ▶He is a retired marine biologist. (他是一名退休的海洋生物学家。)
navigation: ▶Navigation was difficult due to the fog. (由于有雾，航行很困难。) ▶The car has a built-in satellite navigation system. (这辆车配有内置卫星导航系统。)
gulf: ▶There is a wide gulf between the two political parties. (这两个政党之间存在巨大的分歧。) ▶The Gulf of Mexico is prone to hurricanes. (墨西哥湾易受飓风侵袭。)
beach: ▶We spent the day relaxing on the beach. (我们在海滩上放松了一整天。)
coast: ▶They drove along the coast, enjoying the view. (他们沿着海岸开车，欣赏风景。)
shore: ▶We walked along the shore, collecting shells. (我们沿着海岸散步，捡拾贝壳。)
tide: ▶The tide is coming in. (涨潮了。) ▶It takes courage to speak out against the tide of public opinion. (逆舆论潮流而动需要勇气。)
current: ▶Swimmers should be aware of the strong currents. (游泳者应注意强大的水流。) ▶We need to discuss current events in the meeting. (我们需要在会议上讨论时事。)
brook: ▶A babbling brook ran through the forest. (一条潺潺的小溪流过森林。) ▶He would brook no interference in his affairs. (他不能容忍别人干涉他的事务。)
stream: ▶A small stream flowed past the cottage. (一条小溪从小屋旁流过。) ▶The concert was streamed live online. (音乐会在网上进行了直播。) ▶A steady stream of visitors came to the exhibition. (参观展览会的人络绎不绝。)
source: ▶The river's source is a spring in the mountains. (这条河的源头是山中的一处泉水。) ▶Citrus fruits are a good source of vitamin C. (柑橘类水果是维生素C的良好来源。) ▶I need to source some new suppliers for the materials. (我需要为这些材料寻找一些新的供应商。)
shallow: ▶The children were playing in the shallow end of the pool. (孩子们在游泳池的浅水区玩耍。) ▶He has a shallow understanding of the problem. (他对这个问题的理解很肤浅。)
superficial: ▶The wound is only superficial and will heal quickly. (伤口只是表层的，会很快愈合。) ▶She has a very superficial knowledge of art history. (她对艺术史只有非常肤浅的了解。)
flat: ▶The land here is very flat. (这里的地势非常平坦。) ▶The soda has gone flat. (汽水没气了。) ▶He spoke in a flat, emotionless voice. (他用一种平淡、没有感情的声音说话。)
smooth: ▶The surface of the table is very smooth. (桌面非常光滑。) ▶They had a smooth flight with no turbulence. (他们的飞行很平稳，没有遇到气流。) ▶He is a smooth talker. (他是个能说会道的人。)
rough: ▶The rough sea made the boat trip unpleasant. (汹涌的海面使乘船旅行很不愉快。) ▶He gave a rough estimate of the cost. (他给了一个大致的成本估算。) ▶They've had a rough time lately. (他们最近日子不好过。)
sandy: ▶The sandy beach was perfect for building sandcastles. (沙滩是建造沙堡的完美场所。) ▶The soil in this area is quite sandy. (这个地区的土壤沙质很重。)
stony: ▶The path was stony and difficult to walk on. (小路多石，很难走。) ▶He gave me a stony look and refused to answer. (他冷冷地看了我一眼，拒绝回答。)
vertical: ▶The cliff was almost vertical. (那个悬崖几乎是垂直的。) ▶Draw a vertical line down the center of the page. (在页面中央画一条垂直线。)
steep: ▶The path up the mountain was very steep. (上山的路非常陡峭。) ▶There is a steep increase in prices after the festival. (节后价格急剧上涨。)
parallel: ▶The road runs parallel to the railway line. (这条路与铁路线平行。) ▶There are many parallels between the two historical events. (这两起历史事件之间有许多相似之处。)
narrow: ▶The street was too narrow for cars to pass. (街道太窄，汽车无法通过。) ▶They managed to narrow down the list of suspects to three. (他们成功地将嫌疑人名单缩小到三人。) ▶He had a narrow escape from the burning building. (他从燃烧的大楼里死里逃生。)
Oceania: ▶Oceania is a geographic region that includes Australasia, Melanesia, Micronesia, and Polynesia. (大洋洲是一个地理区域，包括澳大拉西亚、美拉尼西亚、密克罗尼西亚和波利尼西亚。)

heating: ▶We turned on the heating because it was cold. (因为天气冷，我们打开了暖气。)

thermal: ▶This jacket is lined with thermal material to keep you warm. (这件夹克内衬保暖材料以保暖。) ▶The region is known for its thermal springs. (该地区以其温泉而闻名。)

moist: ▶Keep the soil moist but not soggy. (保持土壤湿润但不要积水。)

hail: ▶Hailstones the size of golf balls damaged the cars. (高尔夫球大小的冰雹损坏了汽车。) ▶The crowd hailed the returning hero. (人群向归来的英雄欢呼。) ▶Hail from the new intern! (新实习生向你问好！)
thaw: ▶The snow will thaw when the temperature rises. (气温升高，雪就会融化。) ▶Relations between the two countries began to thaw. (两国关系开始解冻。)

freeze: ▶Water will freeze at zero degrees Celsius. (水在零摄氏度会结冰。) ▶The government decided to freeze prices. (政府决定冻结物价。) ▶I froze with fear when I saw the snake. (看到蛇时我吓得呆住了。)
frigid: ▶The frigid air made it difficult to breathe outdoors. (户外的严寒空气让人呼吸困难。) ▶She gave him a frigid stare. (她冷冷地瞪了他一眼。)
tremble: ▶Her hands trembled as she spoke. (她说话时双手颤抖。) ▶The whole house trembled when the train passed by. (火车经过时，整座房子都在震动。)

thunder: ▶We could hear thunder in the distance. (我们能听到远处的雷声。) ▶The tanks thundered through the streets. (坦克轰隆隆地驶过街道。)
lightning: ▶Lightning flashed across the sky. (闪电划破天空。) ▶The decision was made with lightning speed. (决定以闪电般的速度做出。)
stormy: ▶They had to cancel the flight due to stormy weather. (由于暴风雨天气，他们不得不取消航班。) ▶The couple had a stormy relationship. (这对夫妇的关系充满风波。)

biologist: ▶The marine biologist is studying the behavior of dolphins. (这位海洋生物学家正在研究海豚的行为。)

mosquito: ▶Mosquitoes can carry diseases. (蚊子会传播疾病。)

radioactive: ▶The waste from the nuclear plant is highly radioactive. (核电站的废料具有高度放射性。)

invisible: ▶Bacteria are invisible to the naked eye. (细菌是肉眼看不见的。)

presume: ▶I presume you've already eaten. (我猜想你已经吃过了。) ▶We must presume innocence until guilt is proven. (在证明有罪之前，我们必须假定无罪。)
suppose: ▶I suppose you're right. (我想你是对的。) ▶Suppose we leave early to avoid the traffic. (假设我们早点出发以避开交通拥堵。)
hypothesis: ▶The scientist proposed a new hypothesis to explain the results. (科学家提出了一个新的假说来解释这些结果。)
postulate: ▶Einstein postulated that the speed of light is constant. (爱因斯坦假设光速是恒定的。)
speculate: ▶It's useless to speculate about what might have happened. (猜测可能发生了什么是没有用的。)
predict: ▶The weather forecast predicts rain for tomorrow. (天气预报预测明天有雨。)
perceive: ▶Cats are able to see in light levels too low for humans to perceive. (猫能在人类无法感知的低光照下看见东西。) ▶He was perceived as a threat by his rivals. (他被对手视为威胁。)
detect: ▶The test can detect the presence of the virus. (该测试可以检测出病毒的存在。)
discern: ▶It was difficult to discern any pattern in the data. (很难从数据中辨别出任何模式。)
recognize: ▶I recognized her from the photograph. (我从照片上认出了她。) ▶The government recognized the new state. (政府承认了这个新国家。)
conscious: ▶He was conscious of someone watching him. (他意识到有人在看他。) ▶The patient is now fully conscious. (病人现在完全清醒了。)
reckon: ▶I reckon it'll take about three hours. (我估计这要花大约三个小时。) ▶He is reckoned to be the best player in the team. (他被认为是队里最好的球员。)
deem: ▶The area was deemed safe after the inspection. (检查后，该区域被认为是安全的。)
imply: ▶His silence implied agreement. (他的沉默暗示了同意。) ▶Are you implying that I'm lying? (你是在暗示我在撒谎吗？)
deliberate: ▶The jury deliberated for five hours before reaching a verdict. (陪审团审议了五个小时才作出裁决。) ▶The insult was deliberate. (这种侮辱是故意的。)
represent: ▶The red lines on the map represent railways. (地图上的红线代表铁路。) ▶She represents the company in all their legal matters. (她代表公司处理所有法律事务。)
insist: ▶She insisted on paying for her own meal. (她坚持要付自己的饭钱。)
persist: ▶If the pain persists, see a doctor. (如果疼痛持续，要看医生。) ▶He persisted in asking difficult questions. (他坚持问一些难题。)
understand: ▶I don't understand this question. (我不明白这个问题。) ▶It is understood that the fee will be paid in advance. (众所周知，费用将预先支付。)
comprehend: ▶It's difficult to comprehend the sheer scale of the universe. (很难理解宇宙的庞大规模。)
analyse: ▶We need to analyse the data carefully. (我们需要仔细分析数据。)
diagnose: ▶The doctor diagnosed a rare disease. (医生诊断出一种罕见的疾病。)
infer: ▶From his tone, I inferred that he was angry. (从他的语气中，我推断他生气了。)
deduce: ▶From the evidence, we can deduce that he was present at the scene. (从证据中，我们可以推断他当时在场。)
conclude: ▶The report concluded that safety measures were inadequate. (报告得出结论，安全措施不足。) ▶I'd like to conclude by thanking everyone for coming. (最后，我想感谢大家的到来。)
analogy: ▶He used an analogy of a car engine to explain how the heart works. (他用汽车发动机的类比来解释心脏的工作原理。)
compare: ▶Compare the two products before you buy. (购买前比较一下这两种产品。) ▶Her singing has been compared to that of a nightingale. (她的歌声被比作夜莺的歌唱。)
contrast: ▶The white walls contrast sharply with the black floor. (白色的墙壁与黑色的地板形成鲜明对比。) ▶The book contrasts the lives of the rich and the poor. (这本书对比了富人和穷人的生活。)
overlap: ▶There is some overlap between the two theories. (这两种理论有一些重叠之处。) ▶Our shifts overlap by two hours. (我们的班次重叠两个小时。)

disagree: ▶I disagree with you on that point. (在那一点上我不同意你的看法。)
differ: ▶My opinion differs from yours. (我的意见与你的不同。)
diverse: ▶The city has a culturally diverse population. (这个城市拥有文化多元化的人口。)

inductive: ▶Inductive reasoning involves making generalizations from specific observations. (归纳推理涉及从具体的观察中做出概括。)
detail: ▶He explained the plan in great detail. (他非常详细地解释了计划。) ▶The report details the company's financial performance. (报告详细说明了公司的财务业绩。)
thorough: ▶The police conducted a thorough search of the area. (警方对该地区进行了彻底的搜查。)

demonstrate: ▶The salesman demonstrated how the vacuum cleaner works. (售货员演示了吸尘器的工作原理。) ▶The protest demonstrated public opposition to the war. (抗议活动表明了公众对战争的反对。)

manifest: ▶His nervousness was manifest in his trembling hands. (他的紧张表现在颤抖的双手上。) ▶The disease manifested itself in a high fever. (这种疾病表现为高烧。)
prove: ▶Can you prove that you were elsewhere at the time of the crime? (你能证明案发时你在别处吗？) ▶The method proved to be very effective. (这个方法被证明非常有效。)

consonant: ▶B, c, d, f, etc., are consonants. (B, c, d, f等是辅音。)
alphabet: ▶The English alphabet has 26 letters. (英语字母表有26个字母。)
logogram: ▶Chinese characters are a type of logogram. (汉字是一种语标文字。)
vocabulary: ▶Reading is a good way to build your vocabulary. (阅读是积累词汇的好方法。)
dictionary: ▶Look up the word in the dictionary. (在字典里查一下这个单词。)
idiom: ▶"Kick the bucket" is an idiom meaning "to die". ("Kick the bucket"是一个习语，意思是"死"。)
phrase: ▶"On the other hand" is a common phrase. ("另一方面"是一个常用短语。)
clause: ▶A complex sentence contains a main clause and one or more subordinate clauses. (一个复合句包含一个主句和一个或多个从句。)
expression: ▶"It's raining cats and dogs" is a colorful expression. ("下倾盆大雨"是一个生动的表达方式。) ▶Her face wore a sad expression. (她脸上带着悲伤的表情。)
tense: ▶The past tense of "go" is "went". ("go"的过去式是"went"。) ▶I felt tense before the interview. (面试前我感到紧张。)
root: ▶The root of the word "unhappiness" is "happy". ("unhappiness"这个词的词根是"happy"。) ▶The tree's roots go deep into the ground. (树的根深深扎入地下。)
prefix: ▶"Un-" is a prefix meaning "not", as in "unhappy". ("Un-"是一个前缀，意思是"不"，如"unhappy"。)
suffix: ▶"-ness" is a suffix that can form nouns from adjectives, like "happiness". ("-ness"是一个后缀，可以从形容词构成名词，如"happiness"。)
abbreviation: ▶"Dr." is an abbreviation for "Doctor". ("Dr."是"Doctor"的缩写。)
synonym: ▶"Big" and "large" are synonyms. ("Big"和"large"是同义词。)
antonym: ▶"Hot" and "cold" are antonyms. ("热"和"冷"是反义词。)
noun: ▶"Book", "city", and "love" are all nouns. ("书"、"城市"和"爱"都是名词。)
singular: ▶The singular form of "children" is "child". ("children"的单数形式是"child"。)
plural: ▶The plural of "mouse" is "mice". ("mouse"的复数是"mice"。)
pronoun: ▶"He", "she", "it", and "they" are pronouns. ("他"、"她"、"它"和"他们"都是代词。)
verb: ▶"Run", "think", and "be" are verbs. ("跑"、"想"和"是"都是动词。)
adjective: ▶"Red", "happy", and "tall" are adjectives. ("红色"、"快乐"和"高"都是形容词。)
adverb: ▶"Quickly", "very", and "well" are adverbs. ("快速地"、"非常"和"好"都是副词。)
preposition: ▶"In", "on", "at", and "under" are prepositions. ("在...里"、"在...上"、"在"和"在...下"都是介词。)
conjunction: ▶"And", "but", and "or" are conjunctions. ("和"、"但是"和"或者"都是连词。)
consistent: ▶Her work is always of a consistent high quality. (她的工作质量总是稳定地保持在高水平。) ▶Your story is not consistent with the facts. (你的说法与事实不符。)
complicated: ▶The instructions are too complicated to follow. (说明书太复杂，无法遵循。)
complex: ▶It's a complex issue with no easy solution. (这是一个没有简单解决方案的复杂问题。) ▶The new sports complex has a pool and a gym. (新的体育中心有一个游泳池和一个健身房。)
compile: ▶We need to compile a list of all the participants. (我们需要编制一份所有参与者的名单。) ▶The computer compiles the code into an executable program. (计算机将代码编译成可执行程序。)
version: ▶This is the latest version of the software. (这是该软件的最新版本。) ▶He told me his version of events. (他告诉了我他对事件的描述。)
translate: ▶Can you translate this document into French? (你能把这份文件翻译成法语吗？) ▶It's hard to translate my feelings into words. (很难把我的感受用语言表达出来。)
paraphrase: ▶Please paraphrase the paragraph in your own words. (请用你自己的话复述这一段。)
interpret: ▶She will interpret for the foreign delegates. (她将为外国代表做翻译。) ▶How do you interpret his silence? (你如何解读他的沉默？)
narrate: ▶The documentary was narrated by a famous actor. (这部纪录片由一位著名演员解说。)
illuminate: ▶The street lights illuminate the path. (路灯照亮了道路。) ▶His explanation illuminated the complex topic. (他的解释阐明了这个复杂的主题。)
decipher: ▶It took years to decipher the ancient code. (破译这个古老的密码花了好几年时间。) ▶I can't decipher his handwriting. (我辨认不出他的笔迹。)
eloquence: ▶She spoke with great eloquence on the subject. (她在这个问题上讲得非常有说服力。)
communicate: ▶We need to communicate our plans clearly. (我们需要清楚地传达我们的计划。) ▶Dolphins communicate with each other using sounds. (海豚通过声音相互交流。)
discussion: ▶We had a long discussion about the future of the company. (我们就公司的未来进行了长时间的讨论。)
brainstorm: ▶Let's brainstorm some ideas for the project. (让我们为这个项目集思广益。)
debate: ▶There was a lively debate about the new policy. (关于新政策有一场激烈的辩论。) ▶We debated whether to go or stay. (我们辩论了是去还是留。)
commentary: ▶The book provides a commentary on modern society. (这本书提供了对现代社会的评论。) ▶I listened to the live commentary of the football match. (我听了足球比赛的实况解说。)
negotiate: ▶The union is negotiating for higher wages. (工会正在为更高的工资进行谈判。) ▶We negotiated a steep hill in our car. (我们开车爬过了一个陡峭的山坡。)
contention: ▶The border has been a point of contention between the two countries for years. (多年来，边界一直是两国之间的争议点。) ▶It is my contention that we need to invest more in education. (我的主张是，我们需要在教育上投入更多。)


medium: ▶Television is a powerful medium for communication. (电视是一种强大的传播媒介。) ▶She prefers her steak cooked medium. (她喜欢牛排做得中等熟度。) ▶The artist works in various mediums, including oil and watercolor. (这位艺术家使用多种媒介进行创作，包括油画和水彩。)

commentator: ▶The political commentator analyzed the election results on TV. (政治评论员在电视上分析了选举结果。)

apparatus: ▶The laboratory has sophisticated apparatus for experiments. (实验室有复杂的实验设备。)
crane: ▶A crane was used to lift the heavy beams. (用起重机吊起沉重的横梁。) ▶The crane is a large wading bird. (鹤是一种大型涉禽。) ▶She craned her neck to see over the crowd. (她伸长脖子想看到人群上方。)
malfunction: ▶The elevator malfunctioned, trapping people inside. (电梯发生故障，把人困在里面。) ▶A malfunction in the computer system caused the delay. (计算机系统的故障导致了延误。)
maintain: ▶It's important to maintain your car regularly. (定期保养你的汽车很重要。) ▶He maintains that he is innocent. (他坚持自己是无辜的。)
fix: ▶Can you fix the broken chair? (你能修好这把坏椅子吗？) ▶Let's fix a time for our next meeting. (让我们确定下次会议的时间。)
mend: ▶She mended the hole in my sweater. (她补好了我毛衣上的洞。) ▶Relations between the two countries are beginning to mend. (两国关系开始修复。)
modify: ▶We need to modify the design to make it safer. (我们需要修改设计以使其更安全。)
trim: ▶He trimmed the hedge in the garden. (他修剪了花园里的树篱。) ▶The pilot trimmed the aircraft's altitude. (飞行员调整了飞机的高度。) ▶The turkey was served with all the trimmings. (火鸡配以各种配料一起上桌。)
weld: ▶The metal pieces were welded together. (金属件被焊接在一起。) ▶Strong leadership welded the team into a cohesive unit. (强有力的领导使团队凝聚成一个整体。)
saw: ▶He sawed the log into smaller pieces. (他把原木锯成小块。) ▶I saw him yesterday at the store. (我昨天在商店看见他了。)
screw: ▶Use a screw to attach the hinge to the door. (用螺丝把合页固定在门上。) ▶Screw the lid on tightly. (把盖子拧紧。) ▶He really screwed up the project. (他真的把项目搞砸了。)
drill: ▶The dentist drilled my tooth to remove the decay. (牙医钻了我的牙以清除蛀坏部分。) ▶We did a fire drill at school today. (我们今天在学校进行了消防演习。)
plumb: ▶The wall must be perfectly plumb. (墙必须完全垂直。) ▶The book plumbs the depths of human despair. (这本书探究了人类绝望的深渊。) ▶The plumb fixed the leaky pipe. (管道工修好了漏水的管子。)
viaduct: ▶The train passes over the river on a viaduct. (火车通过高架桥过河。)
span: ▶The bridge spans the entire river. (这座桥横跨整条河流。) ▶His career spanned over forty years. (他的职业生涯跨越了四十多年。) ▶The bird has a wide wingspan. (这只鸟的翼展很宽。)
dam: ▶The beavers built a dam across the stream. (海狸在溪流上筑了一座水坝。) ▶The government decided to dam the river for hydroelectric power. (政府决定拦河筑坝以利用水力发电。)

install: ▶We're having a new air conditioner installed tomorrow. (我们明天要安装一台新空调。) ▶She was installed as the new president of the company. (她被任命为公司的新总裁。)
furnish: ▶The apartment is furnished with modern furniture. (公寓配有现代家具。) ▶Can you furnish me with the necessary documents? (你能给我提供必要的文件吗？)
placement: ▶The placement of the furniture makes the room feel larger. (家具的摆放使房间感觉更大。) ▶The agency helps students with job placements. (该机构帮助学生安排工作。)
layout: ▶I like the layout of this website. (我喜欢这个网站的布局。)
design: ▶She studied graphic design in college. (她在大学学习平面设计。) ▶This machine is designed for heavy-duty work. (这台机器是为重负荷工作设计的。) ▶He had designs on her property. (他觊觎她的财产。)
entrance: ▶The main entrance is on the north side of the building. (主入口在大楼的北侧。) ▶Her performance entranced the audience. (她的表演迷住了观众。)
entry: ▶Please use the side entry. (请使用侧门进入。) ▶There were many entries in the photography competition. (摄影比赛有很多参赛作品。)
enter: ▶You must enter the building through the security gate. (你必须通过安全门进入大楼。) ▶He entered the data into the computer. (他把数据输入电脑。)
exit: ▶Please use the emergency exit in case of fire. (如遇火灾，请使用紧急出口。) ▶We exited the highway at the next junction. (我们在下一个路口驶离了高速公路。)
outside: ▶It's raining outside. (外面在下雨。) ▶We need an outside opinion on this matter. (我们需要一个局外人对这件事的看法。) ▶The company outsides some of its work. (公司将部分工作外包。)
outward: ▶The door opens outward. (门向外开。) ▶Despite her outward confidence, she was very nervous. (尽管她外表自信，但内心非常紧张。)
exterior: ▶The exterior of the house needs painting. (房子的外部需要粉刷。) ▶He has a tough exterior but a soft heart. (他外表强硬，但内心柔软。)
external: ▶The medicine is for external use only. (这种药仅供外用。) ▶We need to consider external factors. (我们需要考虑外部因素。)
inner: ▶She struggled with her inner demons. (她与内心的恶魔作斗争。) ▶The inner city has many problems. (市中心有很多问题。)
interior: ▶The interior of the car is very luxurious. (汽车的内饰非常豪华。) ▶She is an interior designer. (她是一名室内设计师。)
inward: ▶The door opens inward. (门向内开。) ▶She turned her inward thoughts into poetry. (她把内心的想法写成了诗。)
internal: ▶The company is conducting an internal investigation. (公司正在进行内部调查。) ▶He suffered internal injuries in the accident. (他在事故中受了内伤。)

ferry 【n.渡船；v.渡运】: ▶We took the ferry to the island. (我们乘渡船去那个岛。) ▶The boat ferries people across the river. (这艘船摆渡人们过河。)
sail 【n.帆；v.航行】: ▶The ship's sails were white. (船帆是白色的。) ▶We sail for France tomorrow. (我们明天启航前往法国。)
raft 【n.木筏；v.乘筏】: ▶They built a raft to cross the river. (他们造了一个木筏过河。) ▶We went rafting down the river. (我们乘木筏顺流而下。)
canoe 【n.独木舟；v.划独木舟】: ▶We paddled a canoe across the lake. (我们划着独木舟穿过湖泊。) ▶They go canoeing every summer. (他们每年夏天都去划独木舟。)
oar 【n.桨；橹】: ▶Each rower pulled hard on their oars. (每个划手都用力划桨。)
deck 【n.甲板；层面】: ▶Passengers were walking on the deck. (乘客们在甲板上散步。)
turbine 【n.涡轮机】: ▶The power station uses steam turbines to generate electricity. (发电站使用蒸汽涡轮机发电。)
propeller 【n.螺旋桨；推进器】: ▶The airplane's propeller started to spin. (飞机的螺旋桨开始旋转。)
stern 【n.船尾；adj.严厉的】: ▶The captain stood on the stern. (船长站在船尾。) ▶The teacher gave him a stern look. (老师严厉地看了他一眼。)
aboard 【adv.&prep.在船上；在车上；上船】: ▶Welcome aboard the flight to Paris. (欢迎乘坐本次飞往巴黎的航班。) ▶He climbed aboard the train. (他登上了火车。)
embark 【v.上船；登机；开始】: ▶We embarked at Southampton. (我们在南安普顿登船。) ▶The company is embarking on a new project. (公司正在开始一个新项目。)
channel 【n.频道；海峡；渠道；v.引导】: ▶Change the channel, please. (请换台。) ▶They channeled the water into the fields. (他们把水引到田里。)
canal 【n.运河；水道】: ▶The Suez Canal connects the Mediterranean Sea to the Red Sea. (苏伊士运河连接地中海和红海。)
ditch 【n.沟；渠；v.抛弃】: ▶The car skidded and ended up in a ditch. (汽车打滑，最后掉进了沟里。) ▶He ditched his old car. (他抛弃了他的旧车。)
railroad 【n.铁路】: ▶The transcontinental railroad changed America. (横贯大陆的铁路改变了美国。)
railway 【n.铁路；铁道】: ▶The railway line runs along the coast. (铁路线沿着海岸延伸。)
locomotive 【n.火车头；机车】: ▶The steam locomotive is now in a museum. (那台蒸汽机车现在在博物馆里。)
subway 【n.地铁；地下通道】: ▶She takes the subway to work. (她乘地铁上班。)
underground 【n.地铁；adj.地下的；adv.在地下】: ▶We traveled by underground. (我们乘地铁出行。) ▶There is an underground car park. (有一个地下停车场。) ▶Rabbits live underground. (兔子住在地下。)
tunnel 【n.隧道；地道；v.挖隧道】: ▶The train went through a long tunnel. (火车穿过一条长长的隧道。) ▶The prisoners tunneled their way out of the jail. (囚犯们挖地道越狱。)
rail 【n.横杆；栏杆；铁轨】: ▶Hold onto the rail when going down the stairs. (下楼梯时扶住栏杆。)
depart 【v.离开；出发】: ▶The train departs from platform 3. (火车从3号站台出发。)
arrive 【v.到达；抵达】: ▶We arrived at the airport two hours early. (我们提前两小时到达机场。)
destination 【n.目的地；终点】: ▶Our final destination is Rome. (我们的最终目的地是罗马。)
delay 【n.&v.耽搁；延迟】: ▶The flight was subject to a long delay. (航班长时间延误。) ▶Fog delayed the landing. (大雾延误了降落。)
postpone 【v.推迟；延期】: ▶They postponed the meeting until next week. (他们把会议推迟到下周。)
defer 【v.推迟；延期；遵从】: ▶The decision has been deferred until next month. (决定被推迟到下个月。) ▶I defer to your greater experience in this matter. (在这件事上，我听从你更丰富的经验。)
lull 【n.间歇；暂停；v.使安静】: ▶There was a lull in the conversation. (谈话中出现了一段间歇。) ▶The mother lulled the baby to sleep. (母亲哄婴儿入睡。)
expire 【v.期满；失效；死亡】: ▶My passport expires next month. (我的护照下个月到期。)
due 【adj.到期的；预期的；应得的】: ▶The rent is due on the first of the month. (房租应在每月一号支付。) ▶The train is due in five minutes. (火车预计五分钟后到达。)
postage 【n.邮费；邮资】: ▶What is the postage for a letter to Australia? (寄往澳大利亚的信要多少邮资？)
stamp 【n.邮票；印章；v.跺脚；盖章】: ▶I need to buy some stamps. (我需要买些邮票。) ▶He stamped his foot in anger. (他气得直跺脚。)
envelope 【n.信封】: ▶She sealed the envelope and mailed it. (她封好信封，然后寄了出去。)
mail 【n.邮件；邮政；v.邮寄】: ▶Is there any mail for me? (有我的邮件吗？) ▶I will mail the documents tomorrow. (我明天会把文件寄出去。)
packet 【n.小包；小袋；数据包】: ▶He gave me a packet of biscuits. (他给了我一包饼干。)
package 【n.包裹；包；v.打包】: ▶A package arrived for you today. (今天有你的一个包裹。) ▶The software is packaged with a manual. (软件附带手册一起包装。)
bind 【v.捆绑；装订；约束】: ▶They bound his hands together. (他们把他的双手绑在一起。)
parcel 【n.包裹；v.分配】: ▶I'm going to the post office to send this parcel. (我要去邮局寄这个包裹。) ▶The land was parcelled out to the farmers. (土地被分配给了农民。)
load 【n.负荷；负载；v.装载】: ▶The truck was carrying a heavy load. (卡车载着重物。) ▶We need to load the car. (我们需要把东西装上车。)
burden 【n.负担；重负；v.使负重】: ▶The debt was a heavy burden on the family. (债务是家庭的沉重负担。) ▶I don't want to burden you with my problems. (我不想用我的问题来加重你的负担。)
transfer 【v.&n.转移；调动；转乘】: ▶He transferred the money to my account. (他把钱转到了我的账户上。) ▶The transfer at the station was quick. (在车站的换乘很快。)
transmit 【v.传输；传送；发射】: ▶The radio station transmits 24 hours a day. (这家电台每天24小时广播。)
transit 【n.运输；经过；v.经过】: ▶The goods were damaged in transit. (货物在运输途中受损了。)
deliver 【v.递送；交付；发表】: ▶The mailman delivers letters every morning. (邮递员每天早晨送信。)
convey 【v.传达；运输】: ▶Words cannot convey my gratitude. (言语无法表达我的感激之情。)
speed 【n.速度；迅速；v.加速】: ▶The car was traveling at high speed. (汽车正高速行驶。) ▶He sped down the road. (他沿路疾驰而去。)
velocity 【n.速度；速率】: ▶The velocity of light is constant. (光速是恒定的。)
swift 【adj.迅速的；敏捷的】: ▶He gave a swift reply. (他迅速作出了答复。)


republic 【n.共和国；共和政体】: ▶China is a people's democratic republic. (中国是一个人民民主共和国。)

government 【n.政府；政体；管辖】: ▶The government is implementing new policies to boost the economy. (政府正在实施新政策以刺激经济。)
authority 【n.权力；权威；当局】: ▶She speaks with an air of authority. (她说话带着一种权威的口吻。) ▶You need to report this to the local authorities. (你需要向地方当局报告此事。)
political 【adj.政治的；政党的】: ▶He decided to pursue a political career. (他决定从政。)
hierarchy 【n.等级制度；统治集团】: ▶The company has a very strict hierarchy. (这家公司有非常严格的等级制度。)
democracy 【n.民主；民主国家】: ▶Freedom of speech is a fundamental principle of democracy. (言论自由是民主的基本原则。)
bureaucracy 【n.官僚制度；官僚作风】: ▶The application process was slowed down by excessive bureaucracy. (申请过程因过多的官僚作风而放缓。)
egalitarian 【adj.平等主义的；n.平等主义者】: ▶Their society is based on egalitarian principles. (他们的社会建立在平等主义原则之上。)
materialism 【n.唯物主义；物质主义】: ▶Modern consumer society is often criticized for its materialism. (现代消费社会常因物质主义而受到批评。)
revolution 【n.革命；巨变；旋转】: ▶The Industrial Revolution changed the world profoundly. (工业革命深刻地改变了世界。)
reform 【n.&v.改革；改良】: ▶The government introduced economic reforms. (政府推行了经济改革。) ▶They are trying to reform the education system. (他们正试图改革教育体系。)
process 【n.过程；进程；v.处理；加工】: ▶Learning a language is a long process. (学习语言是一个漫长的过程。) ▶It will take a week to process your application. (处理你的申请需要一周时间。)
conservative 【adj.保守的；守旧的；n.保守者】: ▶He has very conservative views on social issues. (他在社会问题上观点非常保守。) ▶The conservatives opposed the new law. (保守派反对新法律。)
meltdown 【n.彻底垮台；崩溃；熔毁】: ▶The company is facing a financial meltdown. (这家公司正面临金融崩溃。)
municipal 【adj.市的；市政的】: ▶The municipal government is responsible for local parks and libraries. (市政府负责当地的公园和图书馆。)
neutral 【adj.中立的；中立国的；n.中立国】: ▶Switzerland remained neutral during the war. (瑞士在战争期间保持中立。)

arena 【n.竞技场；活动场所】: ▶The team entered the sports arena. (队伍进入了体育场。) ▶She is a new star in the political arena. (她是政治舞台上一颗新星。)
flag 【n.旗帜；v.标示；疲乏】: ▶The national flag was flying high. (国旗高高飘扬。) ▶Please flag the important emails for follow-up. (请标记重要的邮件以便跟进。)
banner 【n.横幅；旗帜】: ▶Protesters carried banners with slogans. (抗议者举着带有标语的横幅。)

office 【n.办公室；处；官职】: ▶She left her bag in the office. (她把包落在办公室了。) ▶He held the office of mayor for ten years. (他担任市长职务十年。)

dominate 【v.支配；控制；占优势】: ▶The castle dominates the skyline of the town. (城堡俯瞰着整个城镇的天际线。)
power 【n.权力；力量；电力；v.给…提供动力】: ▶The president has the power to veto bills. (总统有权否决议案。) ▶The aircraft is powered by two jet engines. (这架飞机由两台喷气发动机提供动力。)
influence 【n.&v.影响；作用】: ▶His writings have had a great influence on many people. (他的作品对许多人产生了巨大影响。) ▶Don't let me influence your decision. (不要让我影响你的决定。)

importance 【n.重要性；重要】: ▶They stressed the importance of a good education. (他们强调了良好教育的重要性。)
significance 【n.意义；重要性；意思】: ▶The discovery is of great scientific significance. (这一发现具有重大的科学意义。)

liberty 【n.自由；自由权】: ▶The right to liberty is a basic human right. (自由权是一项基本人权。)

slum 【n.贫民窟；v.访问贫民区】: ▶He grew up in the slums of Mumbai. (他在孟买的贫民窟长大。) ▶The journalist spent a month slumming in the city. (这位记者花了一个月时间探访该市的贫民区。)
refuge 【n.避难；庇护；避难所】: ▶During the flood, the school provided refuge for the victims. (洪水期间，学校为灾民提供了避难所。)
asylum 【n.政治避难；庇护；精神病院】: ▶He sought asylum in a foreign embassy. (他在外国大使馆寻求政治庇护。)
population 【n.人口；种群】: ▶What is the population of this city? (这个城市的人口是多少？)
demographic 【adj.人口统计的；n.人口群体】: ▶The study looked at various demographic trends. (这项研究考察了各种人口统计趋势。) ▶This product is aimed at a younger demographic. (这款产品的目标人群是较年轻的群体。)
citizen 【n.公民；市民】: ▶She is a citizen of both Canada and the UK. (她是加拿大和英国的双重公民。)
resident 【n.居民；住客；adj.居住的】: ▶The hotel offers a discount for its residents. (该酒店为住客提供折扣。) ▶She is a resident doctor at the local hospital. (她是当地医院的住院医生。)
ethnic 【adj.种族的；民族的】: ▶The city is home to many different ethnic groups. (这个城市是许多不同种族群体的家园。)
racial 【adj.种族的；人种的】: ▶They are campaigning for racial equality. (他们正在为种族平等而奔走。)
clan 【n.氏族；宗族；大家庭】: ▶The whole clan gathers for Christmas every year. (整个家族每年圣诞节都会团聚。)
franchise 【n.选举权；特许经营权；v.给…以特许权】: ▶Women did not get the franchise until the early 20th century. (妇女直到20世纪初才获得选举权。) ▶He runs a fast-food franchise. (他经营着一家快餐特许加盟店。)
entitle 【v.给…权利；给…题名】: ▶This ticket entitles you to a free drink. (凭此票你可免费获得一杯饮料。) ▶He read a book entitled 'The Great Gatsby'. (他读了一本名为《了不起的盖茨比》的书。)
preference 【n.偏爱；优先权；喜爱】: ▶Do you have any preference for food? (你对食物有什么偏好吗？)
vote 【n.投票；选票；v.投票；选举】: ▶The result of the vote was close. (投票结果很接近。) ▶Citizens vote to elect their representatives. (公民投票选举他们的代表。)
elect 【v.选举；选择】: ▶Americans elect a president every four years. (美国人每四年选举一次总统。)
respondent 【n.回答者；调查对象；被告】: ▶60% of the respondents agreed with the statement. (60%的调查对象同意这一说法。)
poll 【n.投票；民意调查；v.获得选票】: ▶The latest poll shows the government's popularity has fallen. (最新民调显示政府的支持率下降了。) ▶The candidate polled over 10,000 votes. (这位候选人获得了一万多张选票。)
ambition 【n.雄心；抱负；野心】: ▶Her ambition is to become a CEO. (她的抱负是成为首席执行官。)
nominate 【v.提名；任命；指定】: ▶He was nominated for Best Actor. (他获得最佳男主角提名。)
checklist 【n.清单；检查表】: ▶Use this checklist to ensure you have packed everything. (用这张清单检查一下你是否把所有东西都打包了。)
succession 【n.连续；继任；继承权】: ▶He took over the job in succession to his father. (他接替了他父亲的工作。) ▶A succession of accidents spoiled the event. (一连串的事故搞砸了这次活动。)
safety 【n.安全；安全性】: ▶The safety of the passengers is our main concern. (乘客的安全是我们主要关心的问题。)
welfare 【n.福利；幸福；安康】: ▶The company cares about the welfare of its employees. (公司关心员工的福利。)
well-being 【n.健康；幸福；福利】: ◆Yoga can contribute to your overall well-being. (瑜伽有助于你的整体健康。)
harmony 【n.和谐；协调；融洽】: ◆The different groups live together in harmony. (不同的群体和谐地生活在一起。)
steady 【adj.稳定的；稳固的；v.使稳定】: ◆He found a steady job after graduation. (毕业后他找到了一份稳定的工作。) ◆She steadied the ladder while he climbed up. (他爬梯子时，她扶稳了梯子。)
flourish 【v.繁荣；兴旺；茂盛】: ◆The arts flourished during the Renaissance. (艺术在文艺复兴时期蓬勃发展。)
succeed 【v.成功；接替；继承】: ◆If you work hard, you will succeed. (如果你努力工作，你就会成功。) ◆He succeeded his father as CEO. (他接替父亲担任首席执行官。)
prospect 【n.可能性；前景；v.勘探】: ◆The prospect of finding a job soon seems good. (很快找到工作的前景似乎不错。) ◆The company is prospecting for oil in the desert. (该公司正在沙漠中勘探石油。)
perspective 【n.视角；观点；透视图】: ◆The book offers a fresh perspective on history. (这本书提供了一个全新的历史视角。)
viewpoint 【n.观点；看法；视角】: ◆Try to see the issue from a different viewpoint. (试着从不同的角度来看待这个问题。)
standpoint 【n.立场；观点】: ◆From a practical standpoint, the plan is not feasible. (从实际的角度来看，这个计划不可行。)
outlook 【n.观点；展望；前景】: ◆He has a very positive outlook on life. (他对生活有着非常积极的态度。) ◆The economic outlook is improving. (经济前景正在改善。)
guideline 【n.指导方针；准则】: ◆Please follow the safety guidelines. (请遵守安全指南。)
ethic 【n.道德标准；伦理】: ◆The doctor has a strong work ethic. (这位医生有很强的职业道德。)
suggest 【v.建议；表明；暗示】: ◆I suggest that we leave early. (我建议我们早点动身。) ◆The evidence suggests that he is innocent. (证据表明他是无辜的。)
advise 【v.建议；劝告；通知】: ◆I would advise you to see a doctor. (我劝你去看医生。)
proposal 【n.提议；建议；求婚】: ◆They presented a proposal to the committee. (他们向委员会提交了一份提议。)
hint 【n.暗示；提示；v.暗示】: ◆She gave him a hint about what she wanted for her birthday. (她给了他一个暗示，告诉他自己想要什么生日礼物。) ◆He hinted that he might be leaving. (他暗示他可能会离开。)
declare 【v.宣布；声明；申报】: ◆The company declared bankruptcy. (该公司宣布破产。) ◆You must declare any goods over the duty-free limit. (超过免税限额的物品必须申报。)
affirm 【v.肯定；确认；断言】: ◆The court affirmed the lower court's decision. (法院维持了下级法院的判决。)
claim 【v.&n.声称；要求；索赔】: ◆He claims to have seen a UFO. (他声称看到了不明飞行物。) ◆She filed an insurance claim after the accident. (事故后她提出了保险索赔。)
proclaim 【v.宣告；宣布；声明】: ◆The country proclaimed its independence. (该国宣布独立。)
state 【v.陈述；说明；n.状态；州】: ◆Please state your name and address. (请说出你的姓名和地址。) ◆The building is in a poor state of repair. (这栋建筑年久失修。)
announce 【v.宣布；通告】: ◆They announced their engagement at the party. (他们在聚会上宣布了订婚的消息。)
clarify 【v.澄清；阐明】: ◆Could you clarify what you mean? (你能澄清一下你的意思吗？)
assist 【v.帮助；协助】: ◆A nurse assisted the doctor during the operation. (手术期间一名护士协助了医生。)
aid 【n.&v.帮助；援助】: ◆The country receives foreign aid. (这个国家接受外援。) ◆This device aids hearing. (这个设备有助听力。)
encourage 【v.鼓励；激励；促进】: ◆My teacher always encouraged me to read more. (我的老师总是鼓励我多读书。)
implement 【v.实施；执行；n.工具】: ◆The government will implement the new policy next year. (政府将于明年实施这项新政策。) ◆Stone and bronze implements were found at the site. (在现场发现了石制和青铜制的工具。)
monitor 【v.监控；监测；n.监视器；班长】: ◆Doctors monitored his condition closely. (医生密切监测他的情况。) ◆The teacher appointed her as the class monitor. (老师任命她为班长。)
admit 【v.承认；准许进入】: ◆He admitted that he had made a mistake. (他承认自己犯了一个错误。) ◆This ticket admits one person. (此票只准一人进入。)
African 【adj.非洲的；非洲人的；n.非洲人】: ▶African elephants are larger than Asian elephants. (非洲象比亚洲象大。) ▶He is an African. (他是非洲人。)
European 【adj.欧洲的；欧洲人的；n.欧洲人】: ▶Several European countries use the euro. (几个欧洲国家使用欧元。) ▶She is a European. (她是欧洲人。)
Latin 【adj.拉丁语的；拉丁人的；n.拉丁语】: ▶Latin music is very popular. (拉丁音乐非常流行。) ▶Latin was the language of ancient Rome. (拉丁语是古罗马的语言。)
Jewish 【adj.犹太人的；犹太教的】: ▶They celebrate Jewish holidays. (他们庆祝犹太节日。)
Arabian 【adj.阿拉伯的；阿拉伯人的】: ▶The Arabian Peninsula is rich in oil. (阿拉伯半岛石油资源丰富。)
Portuguese 【adj.葡萄牙的；葡萄牙人的；葡萄牙语的；n.葡萄牙人；葡萄牙语】: ▶He speaks Portuguese fluently. (他能说流利的葡萄牙语。) ▶The Portuguese explored the world in the 15th century. (葡萄牙人在15世纪探索了世界。)
Roman 【adj.古罗马的；罗马的；n.古罗马人】: ▶Roman law has influenced many legal systems. (罗马法影响了许多法律体系。) ▶The Romans built many roads. (古罗马人修建了许多道路。)
Russian 【adj.俄罗斯的；俄罗斯人的；俄语的；n.俄罗斯人；俄语】: ▶I'm learning Russian literature. (我正在学习俄罗斯文学。) ▶She is a Russian. (她是俄罗斯人。)
Spanish 【adj.西班牙的；西班牙人的；西班牙语的；n.西班牙人；西班牙语】: ▶We ate at a Spanish restaurant. (我们在一家西班牙餐馆吃了饭。) ▶Do you speak Spanish? (你说西班牙语吗？)
Swiss 【adj.瑞士的；瑞士人的；n.瑞士人】: ▶Swiss watches are famous for their quality. (瑞士手表以质量闻名。) ▶The Swiss are known for their neutrality. (瑞士人以中立闻名。)
Greek 【adj.希腊的；希腊人的；希腊语的；n.希腊人；希腊语】: ▶I love Greek mythology. (我喜欢希腊神话。) ▶Ancient Greeks made significant contributions to philosophy. (古希腊人对哲学做出了重大贡献。)
Italian 【adj.意大利的；意大利人的；意大利语的；n.意大利人；意大利语】: ▶I had a delicious Italian meal. (我吃了一顿美味的意大利餐。) ▶She is Italian. (她是意大利人。)
soviet 【adj.苏联的；苏维埃的；n.苏维埃】: ▶This is a book about Soviet history. (这是一本关于苏联历史的书。) ▶The word 'soviet' means 'council' in Russian. (“soviet”一词在俄语中是“委员会”的意思。)
Indian 【adj.印度的；印度人的；印第安人的；n.印度人；印第安人】: ▶Indian food is often spicy. (印度食物通常很辣。) ▶Many Indians speak English. (许多印度人说英语。)
Australia 【n.澳大利亚】: ▶Sydney is a large city in Australia. (悉尼是澳大利亚的一座大城市。)
New Zealand 【n.新西兰】: ▶New Zealand is known for its beautiful scenery. (新西兰以其美丽的风景而闻名。)
Canada 【n.加拿大】: ▶Canada is the second largest country in the world. (加拿大是世界第二大国。)
Britain 【n.不列颠；英国】: ▶The Industrial Revolution began in Britain. (工业革命始于英国。)
France 【n.法国】: ▶France is famous for its wine and cheese. (法国以其葡萄酒和奶酪闻名。)
Germany 【n.德国】: ▶Germany is an important economic power in Europe. (德国是欧洲重要的经济强国。)


economy 【n.经济；节约；adj.经济的；廉价的】: ▶The country's economy is growing rapidly. (该国经济正在快速增长。) ▶We offer an economy class ticket. (我们提供经济舱机票。)
trade 【n.贸易；行业；v.交易；交换】: ▶International trade is vital for this country. (国际贸易对这个国家至关重要。) ▶He trades in agricultural products. (他从事农产品贸易。)
market 【n.市场；股市；v.销售】: ▶They went to the market to buy fresh vegetables. (他们去市场买新鲜蔬菜。) ▶The company markets its products worldwide. (这家公司在全球销售其产品。)
industry 【n.工业；产业；勤奋】: ▶The automobile industry is a major employer. (汽车工业是主要的雇主。) ▶His success was due to his industry. (他的成功归功于他的勤奋。)
merchant 【n.商人；批发商；adj.商船的】: ▶A wealthy merchant donated the land for the park. (一位富商捐赠了公园的土地。) ▶a merchant ship (商船)
financial 【adj.财政的；金融的】: ▶He is in need of financial assistance. (他需要财政援助。)
fund 【n.基金；资金；v.资助】: ▶The university set up a scholarship fund. (大学设立了一项奖学金基金。) ▶The project is funded by the government. (该项目由政府资助。)
donate 【v.捐赠；捐献】: ▶Many people donated money to the charity. (许多人向该慈善机构捐款。)
endow 【v.捐赠；资助；赋予】: ▶The school was endowed by a local businessman. (这所学校由一位当地商人资助建立。) ▶She is endowed with great musical talent. (她天生具有很高的音乐天赋。)
commercial 【adj.商业的；营利的；n.商业广告】: ▶The project was not a commercial success. (这个项目在商业上不成功。) ▶The TV show was interrupted by commercials. (电视节目被商业广告打断。)
advertise 【v.为…做广告；宣传】: ▶Companies advertise their products on television. (公司在电视上为他们的产品做广告。)
slogan 【n.标语；口号】: ▶"Just do it" is a famous advertising slogan. (“Just do it”是一个著名的广告标语。)
purchase 【v.&n.购买】: ▶The company purchased new computers. (公司购买了新电脑。) ▶She made several purchases at the mall. (她在购物中心买了好几样东西。)
lease 【n.租约；v.出租；租用】: ▶They signed a two-year lease on the apartment. (他们签了一份为期两年的公寓租约。) ▶We lease our car from a local company. (我们从当地一家公司租用汽车。)
afford 【v.买得起；负担得起；提供】: ▶We can't afford a new car this year. (我们今年买不起新车。) ▶The window affords a beautiful view of the garden. (从窗户可以看到花园的美景。)
retail 【n.&v.零售；adv.以零售方式】: ▶The retail price is higher than the wholesale price. (零售价高于批发价。) ▶This product retails for about $20. (这种产品的零售价约为20美元。)
chain 【n.链条；连锁店；一系列】: ▶She wore a gold chain around her neck. (她脖子上戴了一条金项链。) ▶a fast-food chain (快餐连锁店)
grocery 【n.食品杂货；食品杂货店】: ▶I need to go to the grocery store to buy some milk. (我需要去杂货店买些牛奶。)
discount 【n.折扣；v.打折扣；不重视】: ▶Students get a 10% discount. (学生可享受九折优惠。) ▶The store discounted all winter clothing. (商店所有的冬季服装都打折销售。)
promotion 【n.提升；促销；推广】: ▶He got a promotion to manager. (他被提升为经理。) ▶The company is running a special promotion this month. (公司本月正在进行特价促销。)
voucher 【n.代金券；凭证】: ▶I have a voucher for a free meal. (我有一张免费餐券。)
coupon 【n.优惠券；赠券】: ▶She clipped a coupon from the newspaper. (她从报纸上剪下一张优惠券。)
currency 【n.货币；通货】: ▶What currency is used in Japan? (日本使用什么货币？)
exchange 【n.&v.交换；交易；兑换】: ▶We exchanged phone numbers. (我们交换了电话号码。) ▶a stock exchange (证券交易所)
swap 【v.&n.交换】: ▶Let's swap seats so you can see better. (我们换一下座位吧，这样你能看得更清楚。) ▶a book swap (图书交换活动)
receipt 【n.收据；收到】: ▶Please keep your receipt in case you need to return the item. (请保留收据，以防您需要退货。)
invoice 【n.发票；发货清单；v.开发票】: ▶The supplier sent an invoice for the goods. (供应商寄来了货物发票。) ▶We will invoice you for the services provided. (我们将就所提供的服务向你方开具发票。)
tax 【n.税；税款；v.对…征税】: ▶Income tax must be paid by April 15th. (所得税必须在4月15日前缴纳。) ▶Cigarettes are heavily taxed. (香烟被课以重税。)
levy 【v.&n.征收；征税】: ▶The government levies a tax on luxury goods. (政府对奢侈品征税。) ▶a levy on imported goods (对进口商品征收的税)
tariff 【n.关税；价目表】: ▶The government imposed a tariff on foreign steel. (政府对外国钢铁征收关税。)
duty 【n.责任；义务；关税】: ▶It is your duty to report any safety concerns. (报告任何安全隐患是你的责任。) ▶We had to pay customs duty on the imported wine. (我们必须为进口葡萄酒支付关税。)
impose 【v.推行；强制实行；把…强加于】: ▶The school imposes strict rules on attendance. (学校对出勤有严格规定。)
consume 【v.消耗；消费；吃光】: ▶The industry consumes vast amounts of energy. (该行业消耗大量能源。)
spend 【v.用；花；度过】: ▶How much did you spend on groceries? (你买食品杂货花了多少钱？) ▶We spent the weekend at the beach. (我们在海滩度过了周末。)
cost 【n.费用；成本；v.价钱为；使付出】: ▶The cost of living has increased. (生活成本上涨了。) ▶The new equipment costs a lot of money. (新设备花费很多钱。)
expense 【n.花费；开销】: ▶The trip was a business expense. (这次旅行的费用属于业务开支。)
revenue 【n.收入；税收；收益】: ▶The company's revenue increased by 10% this year. (公司今年的收入增加了10%。)
gross 【adj.总的；毛的；严重的；v.获得…总收入】: ▶The gross weight of the package is 5 kg. (包裹的总重量是5公斤。) ▶The film grossed over $100 million. (这部电影获得了超过1亿美元的总收入。)
recession 【n.经济衰退；衰退期】: ▶The economy is in a recession. (经济正处于衰退之中。)
depression 【n.沮丧；经济萧条】: ▶He suffered from depression after the loss. (遭受损失后，他患上了抑郁症。) ▶the Great Depression of the 1930s (20世纪30年代的经济大萧条)
crisis 【n.危机；危急关头】: ▶The government is dealing with an economic crisis. (政府正在处理一场经济危机。)
security 【n.安全；保障；证券；抵押品】: ▶National security is a top priority. (国家安全是重中之重。) ▶She works in securities. (她从事证券业。)
bond 【n.纽带；债券；契约；v.使结合】: ▶The two countries have strong cultural bonds. (两国有牢固的文化纽带。) ▶He invested in government bonds. (他投资了政府债券。)
debt 【n.债务；欠款】: ▶The company is heavily in debt. (这家公司负债累累。)
deficit 【n.赤字；亏损】: ▶The country has a large budget deficit. (该国有庞大的预算赤字。)
inflation 【n.通货膨胀；膨胀】: ▶Inflation is making everything more expensive. (通货膨胀使所有东西都更贵了。)
deflation 【n.通货紧缩】: ▶Deflation can be harmful to an economy. (通货紧缩可能对经济有害。)
dwindle 【v.逐渐减少；缩小】: ▶Their savings dwindled away. (他们的储蓄逐渐减少。)
decrease 【v.&n.减少；降低】: ▶The number of students has decreased this year. (今年学生人数减少了。) ▶a decrease in sales (销售额的下降)
downsize 【v.缩小规模；裁员】: ▶The company had to downsize its workforce. (公司不得不裁员。)
decline 【v.&n.下降；衰退；拒绝】: ▶The population of the town is declining. (这个镇的人口正在下降。) ▶a decline in profits (利润下降) ▶He declined the invitation. (他拒绝了邀请。)
diminish 【v.减少；减小；降低】: ▶The sound diminished into the distance. (声音在远处逐渐消失。)
reduce 【v.减少；缩小；降低】: ▶We need to reduce our expenses. (我们需要减少开支。)
increase 【v.&n.增加；增长】: ▶The price of oil has increased. (石油价格上涨了。) ▶a significant increase in production (产量的大幅增长)
increment 【n.增加；增量】: ▶Salaries are paid in monthly increments. (工资按月支付。)
growth 【n.增长；生长；发展】: ▶The rapid growth of the city has caused problems. (城市的快速发展已经引发了问题。)
escalate 【v.升级；加剧；扩大】: ▶The conflict escalated into a full-scale war. (冲突升级为全面战争。)
expand 【v.扩大；扩展；膨胀】: ▶The company plans to expand its operations overseas. (公司计划将其业务扩展到海外。)
influx 【n.流入；涌入】: ▶The city is preparing for an influx of tourists. (该市正在为游客的涌入做准备。)
affluent 【adj.富裕的；丰富的】: ▶They live in an affluent suburb. (他们住在一个富裕的郊区。)
enrich 【v.使丰富；使富裕；浓缩】: ▶Reading can enrich your life. (阅读可以丰富你的人生。)
sufficient 【adj.足够的；充分的】: ▶We have sufficient evidence to prove his guilt. (我们有充分的证据证明他有罪。)
adequate 【adj.足够的；适当的；差强人意的】: ▶The room was of adequate size. (这个房间大小合适。)
spare 【adj.备用的；多余的；v.抽出；饶恕】: ▶Do you have a spare pen? (你有备用的钢笔吗？) ▶Can you spare a few minutes? (你能抽出几分钟时间吗？)
saving 【n.节省；储蓄；存款】: ▶Switching to LED bulbs leads to energy saving. (换用LED灯可以节省能源。)
redundant 【adj.多余的；被裁减的】: ▶Fifty workers were made redundant. (五十名工人被裁减。)
lack 【n.&v.缺乏；不足】: ▶The project failed due to a lack of funding. (由于缺乏资金，项目失败了。) ▶He lacks confidence. (他缺乏自信。)
company 【n.公司；陪伴；客人】: ▶She works for a software company. (她在一家软件公司工作。) ▶I enjoy your company. (我喜欢有你作伴。)
firm 【n.公司；商行；adj.坚固的；坚定的】: ▶He works for a law firm. (他在一家律师事务所工作。) ▶Make sure the ladder is firm before you climb. (爬梯子前要确保它稳固。)
enterprise 【n.企业；事业；进取心】: ▶Small and medium-sized enterprises are important to the economy. (中小企业对经济很重要。)
agent 【n.代理人；代理商；作用物】: ▶Please contact our agent in London. (请联系我们在伦敦的代理人。)
entity 【n.实体；存在物】: ▶The two companies will combine to form a single entity. (这两家公司将合并成一个实体。)
invest 【v.投资；投入】: ▶It's a good time to invest in the stock market. (现在是投资股市的好时机。)
input 【n.投入；输入；v.输入】: ▶We need more input from the design team. (我们需要设计团队提供更多意见。) ▶Input your password. (输入你的密码。)
product 【n.产品；产物；结果】: ▶The company's main product is smartphones. (该公司的主要产品是智能手机。)
acquisition 【n.获得；收购；获得物】: ▶The museum announced the acquisition of a valuable painting. (博物馆宣布获得一幅珍贵的画作。)
goods 【n.商品；货物】: ▶The store sells a variety of goods. (这家商店出售各种商品。)
cargo 【n.货物】: ▶The ship was carrying a cargo of grain. (这艘船载着一批谷物。)
insure 【v.为…投保；给…保险】: ▶It is wise to insure your house against fire. (为你的房屋投保火险是明智的。)
guarantee 【n.保证；担保；v.保证；担保】: ▶The TV comes with a two-year guarantee. (这台电视机保修两年。) ▶I guarantee that you will be satisfied. (我保证你会满意。)
reliable 【adj.可靠的；可信赖的】: ▶He is a reliable employee. (他是一名可靠的雇员。)
negotiation 【n.谈判；协商】: ▶The price is open to negotiation. (价格可以协商。)
attend 【v.出席；参加；照料】: ▶Will you attend the meeting? (你会参加会议吗？) ▶Nurses attended to the wounded. (护士们照料伤员。)
absent 【adj.缺席的；缺少的；v.缺席】: ▶He was absent from school yesterday. (他昨天没上学。) ▶You should not absent yourself from the important discussion. (你不应缺席这次重要讨论。)
sale 【n.卖；出售；销售额；廉价出售】: ▶The sale of alcohol is forbidden to minors. (禁止向未成年人出售酒精饮料。) ▶The shop is having a clearance sale. (这家商店正在清仓大减价。)
wholesale 【n.批发；adj.批发的；大规模的；adv.以批发方式】: ▶He buys goods at wholesale prices. (他以批发价购买商品。) ▶The company wholesale its products to retailers. (该公司将产品批发给零售商。)
auction 【n.拍卖；v.拍卖】: ▶The painting was sold at auction. (这幅画被拍卖了。) ▶They will auction the antique furniture. (他们将拍卖这些古董家具。)
bid 【v.&n.出价；投标；努力】: ▶She bid $100 for the vase. (她出价100美元买那个花瓶。) ▶Our company made a bid for the contract. (我们公司为这份合同投标。)
deal 【n.交易；协议；v.处理；分配】: ▶We made a deal to share the profits. (我们达成了一项分享利润的协议。) ▶How should we deal with this problem? (我们该如何处理这个问题？)
transaction 【n.交易；业务】: ▶All transactions are recorded. (所有交易都有记录。)
turnover 【n.营业额；人员流动率】: ▶The company has an annual turnover of $5 million. (该公司年营业额为500万美元。)
dump 【v.倾倒；丢弃；n.垃圾场】: ▶It is illegal to dump waste here. (在此倾倒垃圾是违法的。) ▶a rubbish dump (垃圾场)
export 【v.&n.出口；输出】: ▶The country exports crude oil. (该国出口原油。) ▶What are the main exports of your country? (你们国家的主要出口产品是什么？)
import 【v.&n.进口；输入】: ▶We import coffee from Brazil. (我们从巴西进口咖啡。) ▶The import of certain goods is restricted. (某些商品的进口受到限制。)
quota 【n.定额；限额；配额】: ▶The country has a strict immigration quota. (该国有严格的移民限额。)
share 【n.一份；股份；v.分享；分担】: ▶We all have a share in the responsibility. (我们都有一份责任。) ▶She owns shares in the company. (她拥有该公司的股份。) ▶Would you like to share my umbrella? (你愿意和我共用我的雨伞吗？)
benefit 【n.好处；利益；v.有益于；受益】: ▶The new policy will bring benefits to everyone. (新政策将给每个人带来好处。) ▶Who will benefit from this change? (谁将从这个变化中受益？)
interest 【n.兴趣；利息；利益；v.使感兴趣】: ▶She has a great interest in art. (她对艺术有浓厚的兴趣。) ▶The loan carries a high rate of interest. (这笔贷款利率很高。) ▶This new theory interests me greatly. (这个新理论使我很感兴趣。)
dividend 【n.股息；红利；效益】: ▶The company paid a generous dividend to its shareholders. (公司向股东支付了丰厚的股息。)
stock 【n.库存；股票；股份；v.储备】: ▶We have a large stock of these items. (这些商品我们库存很大。) ▶He invested in technology stocks. (他投资了科技股。) ▶The shop is well stocked with fresh fruit. (这家商店备有大量新鲜水果。)
account 【n.账户；描述；解释；v.解释；占】: ▶I have a savings account at the bank. (我在银行有一个储蓄账户。) ▶He gave a detailed account of the incident. (他对事件作了详细的描述。) ▶How do you account for your absence? (你如何解释你的缺席？)
deposit 【n.存款；定金；沉淀物；v.存放；存入】: ▶You need to pay a deposit to secure the booking. (你需要付定金来确认预订。) ▶Please deposit the money into my account. (请将钱存入我的账户。)
installment 【n.分期付款；部分】: ▶We paid for the car in monthly installments. (我们按月分期付款买这辆车。)
cheque 【n.支票】: ▶I will pay by cheque. (我将用支票付款。)
cash 【n.现金；v.兑现】: ▶Do you have any cash on you? (你身上带现金了吗？) ▶Can you cash this check for me? (你能帮我兑现这张支票吗？)
coin 【n.硬币；v.创造】: ▶I need some coins for the parking meter. (我需要一些硬币投停车计时器。) ▶The term "blog" was coined in the late 1990s. (“博客”一词创造于20世纪90年代末。)
shilling 【n.先令】: ▶The shilling was a former unit of currency in Britain. (先令是英国以前的货币单位。)
copper 【n.铜；铜币】: ▶Copper is a good conductor of electricity. (铜是良导体。)
treasure 【n.财富；珍宝；v.珍爱】: ▶The pirates buried their treasure on the island. (海盗把财宝埋在岛上。) ▶I treasure the memories of our time together. (我珍视我们共度的时光。)
wealth 【n.财富；丰富】: ▶He acquired great wealth through his business. (他通过做生意获得了巨额财富。)
estate 【n.地产；财产；庄园】: ▶He owns a large estate in the countryside. (他在乡下拥有一座大庄园。)
possess 【v.拥有；具有】: ▶He possesses great courage. (他拥有巨大的勇气。)
legacy 【n.遗产；遗留物】: ▶He left a legacy to his grandchildren. (他给他的孙辈留下了一笔遗产。)
descend 【v.下来；下降；传下】: ▶The path descends to the valley. (小路向下通到山谷。) ▶This custom descends from ancient times. (这个习俗是古代传下来的。)
worthy 【adj.值得的；有价值的】: ▶This book is worthy of your attention. (这本书值得你关注。)
valuable 【adj.贵重的；有价值的】: ▶She keeps her valuable jewelry in a safe. (她把贵重的珠宝放在保险箱里。)
cheap 【adj.便宜的；廉价的；劣质的】: ▶Fruits are cheap in summer. (夏天水果很便宜。)
incentive 【n.刺激；动机；鼓励】: ▶The company offers financial incentives for good performance. (公司为表现良好者提供金钱奖励。)
accelerate 【v.加速；促进】: ▶The car accelerated rapidly. (汽车迅速加速。)
prompt 【adj.迅速的；及时的；v.促使；提示】: ▶Thank you for your prompt reply. (感谢您的及时回复。) ▶What prompted you to change your mind? (是什么促使你改变了主意？)
salary 【n.薪水】: ▶She earns a high salary. (她薪水很高。)
income 【n.收入；收益】: ▶What is your annual income? (你的年收入是多少？)
wage 【n.工资】: ▶He earns a good wage. (他工资很高。)
payment 【n.支付；付款；支付的款项】: ▶Payment can be made by credit card. (可以用信用卡支付。)
refund 【n.退款；v.退还】: ▶I asked for a refund because the product was faulty. (因为产品有瑕疵，我要求退款。) ▶The store refunded my money. (商店退了我的钱。)
reimburse 【v.报销；偿还】: ▶The company will reimburse your travel expenses. (公司将报销你的差旅费。)
payroll 【n.工资名单；工薪总额】: ▶The company has 500 people on its payroll. (该公司雇用了500人。)
remuneration 【n.报酬；酬金】: ▶The job offers an attractive remuneration package. (这份工作提供诱人的薪酬方案。)
subsidy 【n.补贴；津贴】: ▶The farm receives a subsidy from the government. (该农场获得政府补贴。)
earn 【v.赚得；获得】: ▶He earns a living as a teacher. (他当老师谋生。)
undertaking 【n.事业；企业；承诺】: ▶Starting a business is a risky undertaking. (创业是一项有风险的事业。)
career 【n.生涯；职业】: ▶She has had a successful career in medicine. (她在医学领域事业有成。)
profession 【n.职业；行业】: ▶Teaching is a rewarding profession. (教书是一个有意义的职业。)
occupation 【n.职业；工作；占领】: ▶Please state your name and occupation. (请说出你的姓名和职业。)
job 【n.工作；职位；零活】: ▶He found a job in a bank. (他在银行找到一份工作。)
vocation 【n.天职；使命；行业】: ▶She felt that nursing was her vocation. (她觉得护理工作是她的天职。)
labour 【n.劳动；劳动力；分娩；v.劳动；努力】: ▶The project requires a lot of manual labour. (这个项目需要大量体力劳动。) ▶We laboured all day to finish the work. (我们干了一整天来完成这项工作。)
workforce 【n.劳动力；员工总数】: ▶The company has a highly skilled workforce. (该公司拥有技术娴熟的劳动力。)
workaholic 【n.工作狂】: ▶He is a workaholic who never takes a vacation. (他是个从不休假的工作狂。)
personnel 【n.人员；员工；人事部门】: ▶All personnel must attend the safety meeting. (所有员工都必须参加安全会议。)
clerk 【n.职员；店员；文书】: ▶She works as a clerk in a government office. (她在政府机关当职员。)
interview 【n.&v.面试；采访；面谈】: ▶I have a job interview tomorrow. (我明天有个工作面试。) ▶The journalist interviewed the president. (记者采访了总统。)
resume 【n.简历；摘要；v.重新开始】: ▶Please send your resume to the HR department. (请将你的简历寄给人力资源部。) ▶We will resume the meeting after lunch. (午饭后我们将继续开会。)
recommend 【v.推荐；建议】: ▶Can you recommend a good restaurant? (你能推荐一家好餐馆吗？)
employ 【v.雇用；使用】: ▶The factory employs over a thousand workers. (这家工厂雇用了上千名工人。)
hire 【v.&n.租用；雇用】: ▶We need to hire a new secretary. (我们需要雇一名新秘书。) ▶The car is for hire. (这辆车供出租。)
fire 【v.解雇；开枪；n.火】: ▶He was fired for being late repeatedly. (他因屡次迟到而被解雇。) ▶The soldiers were ordered to fire. (士兵们奉命开枪。)
lay-off 【n.解雇；裁员】: ▶The factory announced another round of lay-offs. (工厂宣布了新一轮的裁员。)
dismiss 【v.解雇；解散；不予考虑】: ▶The manager dismissed the employee for incompetence. (经理以不称职为由解雇了那名员工。) ▶The judge dismissed the case. (法官驳回了此案。)
discharge 【v.&n.排出；解雇；放电；履行】: ▶The factory discharges waste into the river. (工厂将废水排入河中。) ▶He was discharged from the army. (他从军队退伍了。)
resign 【v.辞职；放弃】: ▶She resigned from her position as director. (她辞去了主管的职务。)
sack 【v.解雇；n.大袋】: ▶He got sacked for stealing. (他因偷窃被解雇了。)
retire 【v.退休；退职】: ▶My father will retire next year. (我父亲明年退休。)
result 【n.结果；成果；v.导致】: ▶The exam results will be announced next week. (考试结果将于下周公布。) ▶The accident resulted in two deaths. (事故导致两人死亡。)
failure 【n.失败；故障；不及格】: ▶The project was a complete failure. (这个项目彻底失败了。)
abortion 【n.流产；堕胎；中止】: ▶The law on abortion is controversial. (关于堕胎的法律是有争议的。)
loss 【n.损失；丧失；失败】: ▶The company reported a loss of $2 million. (公司报告亏损200万美元。)
opportunity 【n.机会；时机】: ▶This job is a great opportunity for you. (这份工作对你来说是个很好的机会。)
chance 【n.机会；可能性；运气】: ▶Is there any chance that you can come? (你有机会来吗？)
choose 【v.选择；挑选；情愿】: ▶You can choose any book you like. (你可以选择任何你喜欢的书。)
change 【n.变化；零钱；v.改变；更换】: ▶There has been a change in the weather. (天气发生了变化。) ▶Do you have change for a ten-pound note? (你能换开十英镑的钞票吗？) ▶She changed her mind at the last minute. (她在最后一刻改变了主意。)
solve 【v.解决；解答】: ▶We need to solve this problem quickly. (我们需要迅速解决这个问题。)
develop 【v.发展；开发；成长】: ▶The company is developing a new product. (公司正在开发一种新产品。)
sustainable 【adj.可持续的；能长期维持的】: ▶We need to find sustainable sources of energy. (我们需要找到可持续的能源。)
improve 【v.改进；改善；提高】: ▶You need to improve your English. (你需要提高你的英语水平。)
manage 【v.管理；经营；设法完成】: ▶She manages a team of twenty people. (她管理着一个二十人的团队。) ▶I finally managed to fix the computer. (我终于设法修好了电脑。)
regulate 【v.管理；控制；调节】: ◆Laws regulate the sale of alcohol. (法律管制酒的销售。)
sanction 【n.制裁；批准；v.批准；制裁】: ◆The UN imposed economic sanctions on the country. (联合国对该国实施了经济制裁。) ◆The government sanctioned the use of force. (政府批准使用武力。)
coordinate 【v.协调；配合】: ◆We need to coordinate our efforts. (我们需要协调我们的努力。)
cooperate 【v.合作；配合】: ◆The two companies agreed to cooperate on the project. (两家公司同意就该项目进行合作。)
collaborate 【v.合作；协作；通敌】: ◆The two professors collaborated on a research paper. (两位教授合作写了一篇研究论文。)


law 【n.法律；法规；规律】: ▶It is against the law to steal. (偷窃是违法的。) ▶the laws of physics (物理定律)
legal 【adj.法律的；合法的】: ▶You should seek legal advice. (你应该寻求法律咨询。)
rule 【n.规则；规定；统治；v.统治；支配】: ▶Please follow the rules of the school. (请遵守校规。) ▶The king ruled for fifty years. (这位国王统治了五十年。)
regulation 【n.规章；法规；管理】: ▶There are strict regulations governing food safety. (有严格的法规管理食品安全。)
item 【n.项目；条款；一件商品】: ▶The next item on the agenda is the budget. (议程上的下一项是预算。)
treaty 【n.条约；协议】: ▶The two countries signed a peace treaty. (两国签署了和平条约。)
agreement 【n.协议；同意；一致】: ▶We have an agreement not to discuss this in public. (我们约定不公开讨论此事。)
charter 【n.宪章；特许状；v.包租】: ▶the UN Charter (联合国宪章) ▶The group chartered a bus for the trip. (该团体为这次旅行包租了一辆公共汽车。)
protocol 【n.礼仪；协议；草案】: ▶Diplomatic protocol must be observed at the meeting. (会议上必须遵守外交礼仪。) ▶a communication protocol (通信协议)
norm 【n.规范；标准】: ▶Short skirts have become the norm. (短裙已成为常态。)
benchmark 【n.基准；标准】: ▶This score became a benchmark for future tests. (这个分数成了未来测试的基准。)
criteria 【n.标准；准则】: ▶What are the criteria for selecting the winner? (评选获胜者的标准是什么？)
standard 【n.标准；水平；adj.标准的】: ▶The work is not up to standard. (这项工作未达到标准。) ▶It's a standard procedure. (这是一个标准程序。)
permit 【v.允许；许可；n.许可证】: ▶Smoking is not permitted here. (此处禁止吸烟。) ▶You need a permit to work here. (你需要许可证才能在这里工作。)
allow 【v.允许；准许】: ▶We do not allow pets in the hotel. (我们不允许宠物进入酒店。)
admission 【n.承认；进入许可；入场费】: ▶His silence was seen as an admission of guilt. (他的沉默被视为承认有罪。) ▶Admission to the museum is free. (博物馆免费入场。)
perform 【v.执行；表演；表现】: ▶The doctor performed the operation successfully. (医生成功地做了手术。) ▶The band will perform live tonight. (今晚乐队将现场表演。)
enforce 【v.实施；执行；强迫】: ▶The police enforce the law. (警察执行法律。)
default 【n.违约；缺省；v.不履行；默认】: ▶The company is in default on its loan. (该公司拖欠贷款。) ▶The program will default to the standard settings. (程序将默认使用标准设置。)
reject 【v.拒绝；排斥；n.次品】: ▶The committee rejected his proposal. (委员会拒绝了他的提议。) ▶The factory sells rejects at a low price. (工厂以低价出售次品。)
constraint 【n.约束；限制；强迫】: ▶Financial constraints prevented us from going. (经济限制使我们无法前往。)
official 【adj.官方的；正式的；n.官员】: ▶This is the official result. (这是官方结果。) ▶A government official will visit the area. (一位政府官员将访问该地区。)
mandatory 【adj.强制性的；义务的】: ▶Attendance is mandatory for all members. (所有成员必须出席。)
potent 【adj.强有力的；有效的】: ▶This is a very potent drug. (这是一种非常强效的药。)
bound 【adj.一定的；受约束的；v.跳跃；n.界限】: ▶You are bound by the contract. (你受合同约束。) ▶The dog bounded towards me. (狗向我跳过来。)
obligation 【n.义务；责任】: ▶We have a legal obligation to pay taxes. (我们有纳税的法律义务。)
court 【n.法院；法庭；球场；v.讨好；追求】: ▶The case will be heard in court next week. (此案将于下周开庭审理。) ▶He courted the favor of the rich. (他讨好富人。)
supreme 【adj.最高的；至上的】: ▶the Supreme Court (最高法院)
enact 【v.制定法律；颁布；扮演】: ▶Parliament has enacted a new law. (议会已颁布了一项新法律。)
legislate 【v.立法；制定法律】: ▶It is hard to legislate against discrimination. (很难立法禁止歧视。)
equity 【n.公平；公正；资产净值】: ▶The company is known for its commitment to equity and diversity. (该公司以其对公平和多样性的承诺而闻名。)
fair 【adj.公平的；相当的；adv.公平地；n.集市】: ▶That's not fair! (那不公平！) ▶She did a fair job. (她做得相当不错。)
just 【adj.公正的；合理的；adv.正好；仅仅】: ▶a just decision (公正的决定) ▶I just saw him. (我刚刚看见他。)
prejudice 【n.偏见；成见；v.使有偏见】: ▶The decision was made without prejudice. (该决定是在没有偏见的情况下做出的。) ▶His past experiences prejudiced him against all lawyers. (他过去的经历使他对所有律师都有偏见。)
discrimination 【n.歧视；辨别】: ▶The law prohibits discrimination on the basis of race. (法律禁止种族歧视。)
accuse 【v.指责；控告】: ▶He was accused of murder. (他被指控犯有谋杀罪。)
sue 【v.控告；起诉】: ▶She is suing the company for damages. (她正在起诉该公司要求赔偿损失。)
prosecute 【v.起诉；检举；继续从事】: ▶The suspect will be prosecuted for fraud. (嫌疑犯将因诈骗被起诉。)
condemn 【v.谴责；判刑；宣告不安全】: ▶The government condemned the terrorist attack. (政府谴责了这次恐怖袭击。)
complain 【v.抱怨；投诉】: ▶She complained about the poor service. (她抱怨服务差。)
boycott 【v.&n.联合抵制】: ▶They boycotted the products from that country. (他们抵制那个国家的产品。) ▶a boycott of the elections (对选举的抵制)
session 【n.会议；一场；一段时间】: ▶The court is in session. (法院正在开庭。)
mediate 【v.调解；斡旋】: ▶A diplomat was sent to mediate between the two sides. (一位外交官被派去在双方之间进行调解。)
plea 【n.恳求；抗辩；借口】: ▶He made a plea for help. (他恳求帮助。) ▶The defendant entered a plea of not guilty. (被告提出了无罪抗辩。)
appeal 【n.&v.呼吁；上诉；吸引】: ▶The charity made an appeal for donations. (该慈善机构呼吁捐款。) ▶The defendant decided to appeal the verdict. (被告决定对判决提出上诉。)
contradict 【v.反驳；与…矛盾】: ▶The witness contradicted the defendant's story. (证人反驳了被告的陈述。)
persuade 【v.说服；劝服】: ▶I tried to persuade him to change his mind. (我试图说服他改变主意。)
controversy 【n.争论；争议】: ▶The new policy caused much controversy. (新政策引起了很大争议。)
whisper 【v.&n.低语；耳语】: ▶She whispered the secret in my ear. (她在我耳边低声说出了这个秘密。) ▶They spoke in whispers. (他们低声说话。)
mutter 【v.&n.咕哝；嘀咕】: ▶He muttered a complaint under his breath. (他低声抱怨。) ▶I heard a mutter of disapproval. (我听到一声表示不满的嘀咕。)
murmur 【v.&n.发出连续低沉的声音；低语】: ▶The stream murmured in the background. (小溪在远处潺潺作响。) ▶There was a murmur of conversation in the room. (房间里有低沉的谈话声。)
silent 【adj.沉默的；寂静的】: ▶The crowd fell silent. (人群安静了下来。)
mute 【adj.沉默的；哑的；v.减弱声音】: ▶He remained mute during the entire interrogation. (他在整个审讯过程中保持沉默。) ▶Please mute your microphone. (请把你的麦克风静音。)
investigate 【v.调查；研究】: ▶The police are investigating the crime. (警方正在调查这起犯罪。)
witness 【n.目击者；证人；v.目击】: ▶Police are appealing for witnesses to come forward. (警方呼吁目击者挺身而出。) ▶Did anyone witness the accident? (有人目击事故吗？)
justify 【v.证明…正当；为…辩护】: ▶Can you justify your actions? (你能证明你的行为是正当的吗？)
reasonable 【adj.合理的；通情达理的】: ▶It's reasonable to assume that he knew about the plan. (有理由假设他知道这个计划。)
suitable 【adj.合适的；适宜的】: ▶Is this movie suitable for children? (这部电影适合儿童看吗？)
judge 【n.法官；裁判员；v.判断；审判】: ▶The judge sentenced him to five years in prison. (法官判处他五年监禁。) ▶You shouldn't judge a book by its cover. (你不应以貌取人。)
fury 【n.狂怒；暴怒】: ▶He flew into a fury when he heard the news. (他听到这个消息勃然大怒。)
trial 【n.审讯；试验；adj.试验的】: ▶The man is on trial for murder. (此人因谋杀罪受审。) ▶a clinical trial (临床试验)
suspect 【v.怀疑；猜想；n.嫌疑犯；adj.可疑的】: ▶I suspect that he is lying. (我怀疑他在撒谎。) ▶The police have arrested a suspect. (警方逮捕了一名嫌疑犯。) ▶His behavior is highly suspect. (他的行为非常可疑。)
sentence 【n.句子；判决；v.判决】: ▶This is a complex sentence. (这是一个复合句。) ▶The judge sentenced him to life imprisonment. (法官判处他无期徒刑。)
arrest 【v.&n.逮捕；拘留；阻止】: ▶The police arrested the thief. (警察逮捕了小偷。) ▶He is under arrest. (他被逮捕了。)
jail 【n.监狱；v.监禁】: ▶He was sent to jail for three years. (他被判入狱三年。) ▶The activist was jailed for his beliefs. (这位活动家因他的信仰而被监禁。)
prison 【n.监狱；牢房】: ▶He escaped from prison. (他从监狱逃跑了。)
confine 【v.限制；禁闭；n.界限】: ▶Please confine your comments to the topic under discussion. (请把你的评论限于正在讨论的话题。)
oversee 【v.监督；监视】: ▶She was hired to oversee the project. (她被雇来监督这个项目。)
supervise 【v.监督；管理；指导】: ▶The teacher supervised the exam. (老师监考。)
restrict 【v.限制；约束】: ▶The law restricts the sale of alcohol. (法律限制酒的销售。)
restrain 【v.抑制；制止；约束】: ▶He could barely restrain his anger. (他几乎无法抑制他的愤怒。)
commit 【v.犯；承诺；委托】: ▶He committed a serious crime. (他犯下了严重罪行。) ▶The government has committed itself to improving healthcare. (政府已承诺改善医疗保健。)
sin 【n.罪恶；罪孽；v.犯罪】: ▶Lying is considered a sin in many religions. (在许多宗教中，说谎被视为一种罪过。) ▶We have all sinned. (我们都有罪。)
crime 【n.罪行；犯罪】: ▶Police are working to reduce crime. (警方正在努力减少犯罪。)
vice 【n.恶习；不道德行为】: ▶Smoking is his only vice. (吸烟是他唯一的恶习。)
bribe 【n.贿赂；v.向…行贿】: ▶The official was accused of taking bribes. (该官员被指控受贿。) ▶He tried to bribe the guard. (他试图贿赂警卫。)
rob 【v.抢劫；剥夺】: ▶They robbed the bank. (他们抢劫了银行。)
pirate 【n.海盗；盗版者；v.盗版；掠夺】: ▶Pirates attacked the ship. (海盗袭击了那艘船。) ▶It is illegal to pirate software. (盗版软件是违法的。)
steal 【v.偷窃；偷偷地做】: ▶Someone stole my wallet. (有人偷了我的钱包。)
thief 【n.小偷；贼】: ▶The thief was caught by the police. (小偷被警察抓住了。)
murder 【n.&v.谋杀；凶杀】: ▶He was convicted of murder. (他被判犯有谋杀罪。) ▶She was murdered in her apartment. (她在自己的公寓里被谋杀了。)
suicide 【n.自杀；自取灭亡】: ▶He committed suicide. (他自杀了。)
deceive 【v.欺骗；蒙骗】: ▶He deceived me into signing the papers. (他骗我签署了文件。)
cheat 【v.欺骗；作弊；n.骗子】: ▶He cheated on the exam. (他考试作弊。) ▶He is a cheat. (他是个骗子。)
fraud 【n.欺诈；骗子】: ▶He was found guilty of fraud. (他被判犯有欺诈罪。)
liar 【n.说谎者】: ▶Don't believe him; he's a liar. (别信他，他是个骗子。)
trap 【n.陷阱；困境；v.使陷入困境】: ▶The mouse was caught in a trap. (老鼠被夹在捕鼠夹里了。) ▶The firefighters were trapped by the flames. (消防员被火焰困住了。)
trick 【n.诡计；花招；v.欺骗】: ▶It was a trick to get our money. (这是一个想骗我们钱的诡计。) ▶He tricked me into giving him the key. (他骗我把钥匙给了他。)
pretend 【v.假装；佯装】: ▶The children pretended to be pirates. (孩子们假装是海盗。)
fool 【n.傻瓜；v.愚弄；欺骗】: ▶I was a fool to trust him. (我真是个傻瓜，竟然相信他。) ▶You can't fool me. (你骗不了我。)
stigma 【n.耻辱；污名】: ▶There is still a stigma attached to mental illness. (精神疾病仍然带有污名。)
confess 【v.承认；坦白；忏悔】: ▶She confessed to the crime. (她承认了罪行。)
conform 【v.遵守；符合；顺从】: ▶All students must conform to the school rules. (所有学生必须遵守校规。)
reconcile 【v.使和解；调停；使一致】: ▶They were finally reconciled after years of arguing. (争吵多年后，他们终于和好了。)
obey 【v.服从；遵守】: ▶Soldiers must obey orders. (士兵必须服从命令。)
succumb 【v.屈服；屈从；死于】: ▶The town finally succumbed to the enemy's attack. (该镇最终屈服于敌人的进攻。) ▶He succumbed to his injuries. (他因伤去世。)
penalty 【n.处罚；罚款；罚球】: ▶The penalty for speeding is a heavy fine. (超速的处罚是重罚。)
fine 【n.罚金；罚款；v.处…以罚金；adj.好的；晴朗的】: ▶I had to pay a parking fine. (我不得不付违章停车罚款。) ▶The company was fined for pollution. (该公司因污染被罚款。) ▶It's a fine day today. (今天天气晴朗。)
mortgage 【n.抵押贷款；v.抵押】: ▶They took out a mortgage to buy the house. (他们申请了抵押贷款来买房子。) ▶The house is mortgaged to the bank. (这房子抵押给了银行。)
ownership 【n.所有权；物主身份】: ▶The ownership of the land is disputed. (这块土地的所有权存在争议。)
copyright 【n.版权；著作权】: ▶The book is protected by copyright. (这本书受版权保护。)
privilege 【n.特权；特殊待遇】: ▶Education should be a right, not a privilege. (教育应该是一种权利，而不是一种特权。)
accredit 【v.授权；认可；委派】: ▶The institution is accredited by the government. (该机构是经政府认可的。)
clue 【n.线索；提示】: ▶The police are looking for clues. (警方正在寻找线索。)
access 【n.通道；机会；v.访问】: ▶The building has access for wheelchairs. (该建筑有轮椅通道。) ▶You can access the data online. (你可以在线访问这些数据。)
anonymous 【adj.匿名的；无名的】: ▶The donation was made by an anonymous benefactor. (这笔捐款是由一位匿名捐助者捐赠的。)
FALSE 【adj.错误的；假的；伪造的】: ▶He gave a false name to the police. (他向警方提供了假名。)
genuine 【adj.真正的；真实的；真诚的】: ▶Is the painting a genuine Picasso? (这幅画是毕加索的真迹吗？) ▶She showed genuine concern. (她表现出真诚的关心。)
procedure 【n.程序；步骤；手续】: ▶What is the procedure for applying for a visa? (申请签证的程序是什么？)
routine 【n.常规；惯例；adj.常规的；普通的】: ▶Exercise is part of my daily routine. (锻炼是我日常活动的一部分。) ▶a routine check (例行检查)
consequence 【n.结果；后果；重要性】: ▶If you break the law, you must take the consequences. (如果你违法，就必须承担后果。)
demand 【n.&v.要求；需要】: ▶There is a great demand for these goods. (对这些商品的需求很大。) ▶The workers are demanding higher wages. (工人们要求提高工资。)
request 【n.&v.请求；要求】: ▶They made a request for help. (他们请求帮助。) ▶I request your presence at the meeting. (我请求您出席会议。)
require 【v.需要；要求；命令】: ▶The job requires a university degree. (这份工作需要大学学位。)
petition 【n.请愿书；诉状；v.请愿】: ▶They signed a petition to save the park. (他们签署了请愿书以保护公园。) ▶The group is petitioning for a change in the law. (该团体正在请愿要求修改法律。)
command 【n.&v.命令；指挥；掌握】: ▶The officer gave the command to fire. (军官发出了开火的命令。) ▶He commands a large army. (他指挥一支庞大的军队。)
instruct 【v.指示；命令；教授】: ▶The manager instructed him to wait. (经理指示他等待。) ▶She instructs students in mathematics. (她教学生数学。)


violence 【n.暴力；猛烈】: ▶The government condemned the violence during the protest. (政府谴责了抗议期间发生的暴力行为。)
conflict 【n.冲突；矛盾；v.冲突；抵触】: ▶The two parties are in conflict over the new policy. (双方在新政策上存在冲突。) ▶His account of the event conflicts with hers. (他对事件的描述与她的相抵触。)
raid 【n.&v.突然袭击；搜查】: ▶The police conducted a raid on the suspect's house. (警方对嫌疑人的房子进行了突然搜查。) ▶Vikings used to raid coastal villages. (维京人过去常常袭击沿海村庄。)
enormity 【n.巨大；滔天罪行】: ▶The enormity of the crime shocked the nation. (这一罪行的滔天程度震惊了全国。)
campaign 【n.运动；战役；v.参加运动】: ▶The company launched an advertising campaign. (公司发起了一场广告宣传运动。) ▶He is campaigning for environmental protection. (他正在为环境保护进行宣传活动。)
battle 【n.战役；斗争；v.斗争】: ▶The battle lasted for three days. (这场战役持续了三天。) ▶She battled against cancer for years. (她与癌症斗争了多年。)
struggle 【n.&v.斗争；奋斗；努力】: ▶The struggle for independence was long and hard. (争取独立的斗争是漫长而艰苦的。) ▶He struggled to lift the heavy box. (他努力抬起那个重箱子。)
explosion 【n.爆炸；激增】: ▶The explosion could be heard miles away. (爆炸声几英里外都能听到。) ▶a population explosion (人口激增)
bombard 【v.轰炸；不断攻击】: ▶The city was bombarded for weeks. (这座城市被轰炸了数周。) ▶The speaker was bombarded with questions. (演讲者遭到了连珠炮似的提问。)
bomb 【n.炸弹；v.轰炸】: ▶A bomb exploded in the city center. (一枚炸弹在市中心爆炸了。) ▶The enemy bombed the bridge. (敌人炸毁了桥梁。)
blast 【n.爆炸；一股；v.爆炸；批评】: ▶Several people were injured in the blast. (几人在爆炸中受伤。) ▶The rock music blasted from the speakers. (摇滚乐从扬声器中轰鸣而出。)
burst 【v.爆炸；爆裂；n.爆发】: ▶The balloon burst with a loud pop. (气球砰的一声爆了。) ▶a burst of laughter (一阵大笑)
spark 【n.火花；v.引发；触发】: ▶Sparks flew from the bonfire. (篝火中飞出火花。) ▶His comment sparked a heated debate. (他的评论引发了一场激烈的辩论。)
twinkle 【v.&n.闪烁；闪耀】: ▶Stars twinkled in the night sky. (星星在夜空中闪烁。) ▶He had a twinkle in his eye. (他眼睛里闪烁着光芒。)

cannon 【n.大炮；加农炮】: ▶Cannons were used in the battle. (那场战役中使用了大炮。)

pistol 【n.手枪】: ▶The officer drew his pistol. (警官拔出了他的手枪。)

bullet 【n.子弹】: ▶A bullet struck the wall. (一颗子弹击中了墙壁。)
target 【n.目标；靶子；v.把…作为目标】: ▶The arrow hit the center of the target. (箭射中了靶心。) ▶The advertisement targets young adults. (这则广告以年轻人为目标。)
deflect 【v.使偏斜；转移】: ▶The shield deflected the arrow. (盾牌挡偏了箭。) ▶He deflected the question skillfully. (他巧妙地回避了这个问题。)
mission 【n.任务；使命；代表团】: ▶His mission was to rescue the hostages. (他的任务是营救人质。)
flame 【n.火焰；v.燃烧】: ▶The flames grew higher. (火焰越烧越高。) ▶Her anger flamed up. (她勃然大怒。)
flare 【v.闪耀；突然爆发；n.闪光信号】: ▶Tempers flared during the argument. (争论中脾气突然爆发了。) ▶The ship fired a distress flare. (那艘船发射了一枚遇难信号弹。)

beat 【v.打；打败；n.敲打；节拍】: ▶He beat the drum loudly. (他用力打鼓。) ▶the steady beat of the heart (心脏有规律的跳动)

punch 【v.用拳猛击；n.一拳】: ▶He punched the wall in frustration. (他沮丧地用拳头猛击墙壁。) ▶a punch in the stomach (打在肚子上的一拳)
chop 【v.砍；劈；n.砍；排骨】: ▶He chopped down the tree. (他砍倒了那棵树。) ▶a lamb chop (羊排)
stab 【v.&n.刺；戳】: ▶The victim was stabbed in the back. (受害者背部被刺。) ▶a stab of pain (一阵剧痛)
dilemma 【n.困境；进退两难】: ▶She faced the dilemma of choosing between her career and her family. (她面临在事业和家庭之间做出选择的困境。)

pitfall 【n.陷阱；隐患】: ▶This book points out the potential pitfalls of starting a new business. (这本书指出了创业可能遇到的隐患。)

savage 【adj.野蛮的；凶猛的；v.猛烈攻击】: ▶a savage attack (凶猛的攻击) ▶The dog savaged the postman. (那条狗猛烈攻击了邮递员。)
reckless 【adj.鲁莽的；不计后果的】: ▶He was arrested for reckless driving. (他因鲁莽驾驶而被捕。)
fierce 【adj.凶猛的；激烈的】: ▶a fierce dog (凶猛的狗) ▶fierce competition (激烈的竞争)
foul 【adj.难闻的；邪恶的；v.犯规】: ▶a foul smell (恶臭) ▶He was fouled by the defender. (他被防守队员犯规了。)
evil 【adj.邪恶的；n.邪恶】: ▶an evil spirit (邪恶的灵魂) ▶the struggle between good and evil (善与恶的斗争)
devil 【n.魔鬼；恶魔】: ▶He was possessed by a devil. (他被魔鬼附身了。)
punishment 【n.惩罚；处罚】: ▶The punishment for murder is life imprisonment. (谋杀罪的惩罚是无期徒刑。)
execute 【v.处决；执行】: ▶The prisoner was executed at dawn. (囚犯在黎明时被处决。) ▶The plan was poorly executed. (这个计划执行得很差。)
hang 【v.悬挂；绞死】: ▶Hang your coat on the hook. (把你的外套挂在钩子上。) ▶In the past, people were hanged for stealing. (在过去，人们会因偷窃而被绞死。)
sacrifice 【n.牺牲；祭品；v.牺牲】: ▶He made many sacrifices for his family. (他为家庭做出了许多牺牲。) ▶She sacrificed her career to look after her children. (她为了照顾孩子而牺牲了自己的事业。)
casualty 【n.伤亡人员；受害者】: ▶There were no casualties in the fire. (火灾中没有人员伤亡。)
bury 【v.埋葬；掩埋】: ▶He was buried in the churchyard. (他被安葬在教堂墓地里。)
funeral 【n.葬礼】: ▶Hundreds of people attended his funeral. (数百人参加了他的葬礼。)
grave 【n.坟墓；adj.严重的】: ▶She visits her mother's grave every week. (她每周都去给母亲扫墓。) ▶a grave mistake (严重的错误)
tomb 【n.坟墓；陵墓】: ▶the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier (无名战士墓)

naval 【adj.海军的】: ▶a naval base (海军基地)

landing 【n.登陆；着陆；楼梯平台】: ▶The landing was successful. (登陆成功了。) ▶a forced landing (迫降)
hover 【v.盘旋；徘徊】: ▶A helicopter hovered overhead. (一架直升机在头顶盘旋。) ▶She hovered nervously in the background. (她紧张地在后面徘徊。)
proceed 【v.进行；继续做】: ▶The meeting proceeded as planned. (会议按计划进行。)
progress 【n.进步；进展；v.进步】: ▶We have made significant progress. (我们取得了重大进展。) ▶Work on the new road is progressing well. (新道路的施工进展顺利。)

risk 【n.危险；风险；v.冒…的风险】: ▶Smoking increases the risk of heart disease. (吸烟会增加患心脏病的风险。) ▶He risked his life to save her. (他冒着生命危险去救她。)

withstand 【v.经受住；抵挡】: ▶These shoes will withstand hard wear. (这些鞋很耐穿。)
compromise 【n.&v.妥协；折衷；危害】: ▶Both sides will have to make compromises. (双方都将不得不做出妥协。) ▶He would never compromise his principles. (他绝不会妥协自己的原则。)

guest 【n.客人；宾客】: ▶We have guests for dinner tonight. (今晚我们有客人来吃晚饭。)
customer 【n.顾客；主顾】: ▶The store values its customers. (这家商店重视它的顾客。)
client 【n.客户；委托人】: ▶The lawyer met with his client. (律师会见了他的委托人。)
encounter 【v.&n.遇到；遭遇】: ▶I encountered an old friend on the street. (我在街上遇到一位老朋友。) ▶a chance encounter (偶然相遇)
chase 【v.&n.追逐；追赶】: ▶The dog chased the cat. (狗追猫。) ▶a high-speed car chase (高速汽车追逐)
miss 【v.未击中；想念；错过】: ▶He shot at the target but missed. (他朝目标射击，但没打中。) ▶I miss my family. (我想念我的家人。) ▶Don't miss the train. (别错过火车。)
appointment 【n.约会；任命】: ▶I have a dentist appointment at 3 pm. (我下午3点有牙医预约。) ▶the appointment of a new manager (新经理的任命)
accompany 【v.陪伴；伴随；为…伴奏】: ▶She accompanied me to the airport. (她陪我去机场。) ▶The singer was accompanied on the piano by her sister. (这位歌手由她妹妹钢琴伴奏。)
dependent 【adj.依靠的；依赖的；n.受抚养者】: ▶She is still dependent on her parents. (她仍然依赖父母。) ▶tax benefits for dependents (给受抚养者的税收优惠)
propose 【v.提议；建议；求婚】: ▶I propose that we start early. (我建议我们早点出发。) ▶He proposed to her on the beach. (他在海滩上向她求婚了。)
engagement 【n.订婚；约会； engagement】: ▶They announced their engagement. (他们宣布订婚了。) ▶a business engagement (商务约会)
marry 【v.结婚；娶；嫁】: ▶They plan to marry next year. (他们计划明年结婚。)
wedding 【n.婚礼】: ▶The wedding will be held in a church. (婚礼将在教堂举行。)
honeymoon 【n.蜜月】: ▶They went to Paris for their honeymoon. (他们去巴黎度蜜月了。)
kiss 【v.&n.吻】: ▶He kissed her cheek. (他吻了她的脸颊。) ▶a goodbye kiss (告别吻)
divorce 【n.&v.离婚；分离】: ▶The divorce rate is increasing. (离婚率在上升。) ▶They decided to divorce. (他们决定离婚。)
separate 【v.分开；分离；adj.分开的；不同的】: ▶The teacher separated the fighting boys. (老师把打架的男孩们分开了。) ▶They have separate bedrooms. (他们有各自的卧室。)
single 【adj.单一的；单身的；n.单程票；单身者】: ▶a single bed (单人床) ▶She is still single. (她还是单身。) ▶a single to London (去伦敦的单程票)
sole 【adj.唯一的；单独的】: ▶She is the sole survivor of the accident. (她是事故的唯一幸存者。)
respective 【adj.各自的；分别的】: ▶They went back to their respective homes. (他们回到了各自的家。)
each 【adj.&pron.每个；各自】: ▶Each student has a book. (每个学生都有一本书。) ▶They each received a prize. (他们各自都得了奖。)
individual 【adj.个别的；独特的；n.个人】: ▶Each individual leaf is different. (每片叶子都是不同的。) ▶the rights of the individual (个人权利)
commuter 【n.通勤者】: ▶The train is full of commuters. (火车上挤满了通勤者。)
neighbourhood 【n.邻近地区；街坊】: ▶It's a quiet neighbourhood. (这是个安静的街区。)

boss 【n.老板；上司】: ▶My boss is very supportive. (我的老板非常支持我。)

supervisor 【n.监督人；导师】: ▶Your supervisor will help you with the project. (你的导师会帮助你完成这个项目。)
subordinate 【n.下属；部属；adj.下级的；从属的】: ▶He treats his subordinates well. (他对待下属很好。) ▶a subordinate clause (从句)
partner 【n.伙伴；合伙人；配偶】: ▶a business partner (商业伙伴) ▶my dancing partner (我的舞伴)
mate 【n.伙伴；同事；配偶】: ▶He's my mate from work. (他是我工作中的伙伴。) ▶a bird looking for a mate (一只寻找配偶的鸟)
colleague 【n.同事；同僚】: ▶I often have lunch with my colleagues. (我经常和同事们一起吃午饭。)
comrade 【n.同志；战友】: ▶They were comrades in the war. (他们是战争中的战友。)
acquaintance 【n.相识的人；了解】: ▶He is a business acquaintance. (他是一位生意上认识的人。) ▶I have some acquaintance with French. (我懂一点法语。)
friendship 【n.友谊；友情】: ▶Their friendship has lasted for years. (他们的友谊已持续多年。)
affection 【n.喜爱；感情】: ▶She has a great affection for her grandchildren. (她非常疼爱她的孙辈。)
stranger 【n.陌生人；外地人】: ▶Don't talk to strangers. (不要和陌生人说话。)
apprentice 【n.学徒；生手】: ▶He started as an apprentice carpenter. (他从木匠学徒做起。)

hero 【n.英雄；男主角】: ▶He was hailed as a hero. (他被誉为英雄。) ▶the hero of the novel (小说的男主角)

committee 【n.委员会】: ▶a special committee (一个特别委员会)

specialist 【n.专家；专科医生】: ▶a heart specialist (心脏病专家)

veterinary 【adj.兽医的】: ▶a veterinary surgeon (兽医)
counsellor 【n.顾问；辅导员】: ▶a marriage guidance counsellor (婚姻指导顾问)
