umpire 【n.裁判员；v.担任裁判】: ▶the umpire in a tennis match (网球比赛的裁判) ▶Who will umpire the game? (谁将担任这场比赛的裁判？)

nurse 【n.护士；v.护理；照料】: ▶a qualified nurse (一名合格的护士) ▶She nursed him back to health. (她护理他直到康复。)
gardener 【n.园丁；花匠】: ▶The gardener is planting flowers. (园丁正在种花。)

butcher 【n.屠夫；肉贩；v.屠宰；残杀】: ▶I bought some meat from the butcher. (我从肉贩那里买了些肉。) ▶The soldiers were butchered by the enemy. (士兵们被敌人残杀了。)
groom 【n.新郎；马夫；v.刷洗；使整洁】: ▶The groom looked nervous. (新郎看起来很紧张。) ▶to groom a horse (刷洗马匹)
hostage 【n.人质】: ▶The terrorists held the passengers hostage. (恐怖分子将乘客扣为人质。)

beggar 【n.乞丐；v.使贫穷】: ▶He gave some money to the beggar. (他给了乞丐一些钱。) ▶The cost of the repairs beggared them. (修理费使他们一贫如洗。)
slave 【n.奴隶；v.苦干】: ▶Slaves were used to build the pyramids. (奴隶被用来建造金字塔。) ▶I've been slaving over this report all night. (我整晚都在拼命写这份报告。)
coward 【n.懦夫；胆小鬼】: ▶He was called a coward for running away. (他因逃跑而被称为懦夫。)


act 【v.行动；扮演；n.行为；法令；一幕】: ▶We must act now to protect the environment. (我们必须立即采取行动保护环境。) ▶She acted in several plays. (她参演过好几部戏剧。) ▶It was an act of great courage. (这是一种非常勇敢的行为。)
behave 【v.表现；举止得体】: ▶The children behaved very well at the party. (孩子们在聚会上表现得很好。)
deed 【n.行为；事迹；契约】: ▶He is remembered for his good deeds. (他因他的善行而被人们铭记。)
accustom 【v.使习惯于】: ▶It took him a while to accustom himself to the new job. (他花了一段时间才适应新工作。)
react 【v.反应；起化学反应】: ▶How did she react to the news? (她对这个消息作何反应？)
respond 【v.回答；响应】: ▶He responded to my question quickly. (他很快回答了我的问题。)
reflect 【v.反映；反射；深思】: ▶Her writing reflects her personality. (她的作品反映了她的个性。) ▶The moon reflects light from the sun. (月亮反射太阳的光。)
bear 【v.承受；忍受；带有；生育】: ▶She couldn't bear the pain. (她无法忍受这种痛苦。) ▶The document bears his signature. (文件上有他的签名。) ▶She bore three children. (她生了三个孩子。)
adopt 【v.收养；采用】: ▶They decided to adopt a child. (他们决定收养一个孩子。) ▶The company adopted a new strategy. (公司采用了新策略。)
nourish 【v.滋养；培育】: ▶Food is needed to nourish our bodies. (我们需要食物来滋养身体。)
mow 【v.割草；刈】: ▶He mows the lawn every Saturday. (他每星期六修剪草坪。)
support 【v.&n.支持；支撑；资助】: ▶I will always support you. (我会永远支持你。) ▶The bridge has strong supports. (这座桥有坚固的桥墩。)
exhale 【v.呼气】: ▶He exhaled slowly. (他慢慢地呼气。)

revive 【v.使苏醒；复兴】: ▶The doctors revived the patient. (医生们使病人苏醒过来。) ▶Efforts to revive the economy are underway. (重振经济的努力正在进行中。)
survive 【v.幸存；活下来；比…活得长】: ▶Few people survived the earthquake. (很少有人在那场地震中幸存。) ▶She survived her husband by ten years. (她比丈夫多活了十年。)
glare 【v.怒目而视；发出强光；n.强光；怒视】: ▶The teacher glared at the noisy students. (老师怒视着吵闹的学生。) ▶the glare of the sun (太阳的强光)
glimpse 【n.&v.一瞥；瞥见】: ▶I caught a glimpse of him in the crowd. (我在人群中瞥见了他。) ▶She glimpsed a figure in the darkness. (她瞥见黑暗中有个人影。)
glance 【v.&n.瞥一眼；扫视】: ▶He glanced at his watch. (他看了一眼手表。) ▶She gave me a quick glance. (她快速地瞥了我一眼。)
peep 【v.&n.偷看；窥视】: ▶He peeped through the keyhole. (他从钥匙孔里偷看。) ▶Let me have a peep at your new phone. (让我偷瞄一眼你的新手机。)
gaze 【v.&n.凝视；注视】: ▶She gazed out of the window. (她凝视着窗外。) ▶His gaze was fixed on the painting. (他的目光固定在画上。)
peer 【v.仔细看；费力地看；n.同龄人；同辈】: ▶She peered at the small print. (她费力地看着小字。) ▶Children are influenced by their peers. (孩子会受到同龄人的影响。)
stare 【v.&n.盯着看；凝视】: ▶It's rude to stare at people. (盯着别人看是不礼貌的。) ▶He gave me an angry stare. (他生气地瞪了我一眼。)
contemplate 【v.沉思；考虑；注视】: ▶She contemplated her future. (她沉思着自己的未来。)
vow 【n.誓言；v.发誓】: ▶They made a vow to love each other forever. (他们发誓永远相爱。) ▶He vowed to get revenge. (他发誓要报仇。)
oath 【n.誓言；宣誓；诅咒】: ▶Witnesses must take an oath to tell the truth. (证人必须宣誓说实话。)
pledge 【n.&v.保证；誓言；抵押】: ▶We made a pledge to help the poor. (我们承诺帮助穷人。) ▶He pledged his support for the campaign. (他承诺支持这项运动。)
whistle 【v.吹口哨；鸣笛；n.口哨；哨子】: ▶He whistled a happy tune. (他吹着一首欢快的口哨曲。) ▶The referee blew his whistle. (裁判吹响了他的哨子。)
reply 【v.&n.回答；答复】: ▶Please reply to my email as soon as possible. (请尽快回复我的邮件。) ▶I am waiting for your reply. (我在等你的回复。)
notify 【v.通知；告知】: ▶The school will notify parents if a student is absent. (如果有学生缺席，学校会通知家长。)
assert 【v.断言；主张；坚持】: ▶She asserted her innocence. (她坚称自己是无辜的。)
explain 【v.解释；说明】: ▶Can you explain how this machine works? (你能解释一下这台机器是如何工作的吗？)
quarrel 【n.&v.争吵；吵架】: ▶They had a quarrel about money. (他们为钱吵了一架。) ▶The children quarrel all the time. (孩子们总是吵架。)
dispute 【n.&v.争论；争端；质疑】: ▶There is a dispute over the ownership of the land. (关于这块土地的所有权存在争议。) ▶I don't dispute his honesty. (我不质疑他的诚实。)
argument 【n.争论；论点；理由】: ▶They had an argument about politics. (他们就政治问题进行了争论。) ▶There is a strong argument for changing the law. (有一个支持修改法律的强有力的理由。)
mention 【v.&n.提到；说起】: ▶He mentioned that he might be late. (他提到他可能会迟到。) ▶He made no mention of her name. (他没有提到她的名字。)
hurry 【v.匆忙；催促；n.匆忙】: ▶We need to hurry if we want to catch the train. (如果想赶上火车，我们得快点。) ▶In his hurry, he forgot his keys. (匆忙中，他忘了带钥匙。)
hasten 【v.加速；赶快】: ▶She hastened to finish her work. (她加紧完成工作。)
urge 【v.敦促；力劝；n.强烈的欲望】: ▶I urge you to reconsider your decision. (我力劝你重新考虑你的决定。) ▶He felt a sudden urge to travel. (他突然有一股想去旅行的强烈欲望。)
scold 【v.责骂；训斥】: ▶The mother scolded her child for running into the street. (母亲因孩子跑到街上而责骂他。)
curse 【v.&n.诅咒；咒骂】: ▶He cursed when he dropped the hammer on his foot. (当锤子砸到他的脚时，他咒骂了一句。) ▶The witch put a curse on the prince. (女巫对王子下了诅咒。)
swear 【v.发誓；诅咒；咒骂】: ▶I swear I will tell the truth. (我发誓我会说实话。) ▶He swore loudly at the other driver. (他对着另一个司机大声咒骂。)
provoke 【v.挑衅；激怒；引起】: ▶His rude remarks provoked her anger. (他粗鲁的言论激怒了她。)
preach 【v.布道；宣扬；说教】: ▶The priest preached a sermon about forgiveness. (神父宣讲了一篇关于宽恕的布道文。)
boast 【v.&n.自夸；夸耀】: ▶He boasted about his wealth. (他夸耀自己的财富。) ▶It was her proud boast that she had never been late. (她从未迟到过，这是她引以为豪的事。)
tease 【v.&n.取笑；戏弄；逗弄】: ▶The other children teased him about his glasses. (其他孩子取笑他的眼镜。) ▶Don't get upset; it was just a tease. (别生气，只是开玩笑而已。)
mock 【v.嘲笑；模仿；adj.模拟的；假的】: ▶The other students mocked his accent. (其他学生嘲笑他的口音。) ▶a mock exam (模拟考试)
touch 【v.触摸；接触；感动；n.触觉；接触】: ▶Do not touch the wet paint. (请勿触摸未干的油漆。) ▶The story touched my heart. (这个故事触动了我的心。) ▶I felt a light touch on my shoulder. (我感到有人轻轻碰了下我的肩膀。)
hug 【v.&n.拥抱】: ▶She hugged her friend goodbye. (她拥抱朋友告别。) ▶He gave me a big hug. (他给了我一个紧紧的拥抱。)
tap 【v.轻拍；轻敲；n.水龙头；轻敲】: ▶He tapped me on the shoulder. (他轻轻拍了拍我的肩膀。) ▶Please turn off the tap. (请关掉水龙头。)
clap 【v.拍手；鼓掌；n.拍手声】: ▶The audience clapped enthusiastically. (观众热烈鼓掌。) ▶a clap of thunder (一声雷鸣)
applaud 【v.鼓掌；称赞】: ▶The crowd applauded the performers. (人群为表演者鼓掌。)
kneel 【v.跪下】: ▶He knelt down to tie his shoe. (他蹲下来系鞋带。)
catch 【v.抓住；赶上；染上；n.捕获物】: ▶Catch the ball! (接球！) ▶I need to catch the 8 o'clock train. (我需要赶上8点的火车。) ▶a good catch of fish (捕获的大量鱼)
snatch 【v.夺走；抢；n.片段】: ▶The thief snatched her purse and ran away. (小偷抢了她的钱包就跑。) ▶I only heard snatches of their conversation. (我只听到他们谈话的片段。)
grab 【v.抓住；攫取；n.抓取】: ▶He grabbed my arm to stop me from falling. (他抓住我的胳膊，防止我摔倒。)
grasp 【v.抓紧；理解；n.抓；理解】: ▶Grasp the rope tightly. (抓紧绳子。) ▶I couldn't grasp the meaning of his words. (我无法理解他话中的含义。) ▶She has a good grasp of the subject. (她对这门学科掌握得很好。)
overtake 【v.追上；超过；突然降临】: ▶It's dangerous to overtake on a bend. (在弯道超车是危险的。) ▶A sudden storm overtook us. (我们突然遭遇了暴风雨。)
follow 【v.跟随；遵循；理解】: ▶Please follow me. (请跟我来。) ▶Follow the instructions carefully. (仔细遵循说明。) ▶I couldn't follow his argument. (我听不懂他的论点。)
grip 【v.紧握；紧抓；n.紧握；控制】: ▶Grip the handle firmly. (紧紧抓住把手。) ▶He has a strong grip. (他握力很大。) ▶The country is in the grip of a recession. (该国正处在经济衰退中。)
mess 【n.杂乱；肮脏；v.弄乱；搞糟】: ▶Your room is a mess! (你的房间一团糟！) ▶Don't mess up my plans. (别打乱我的计划。)
twist 【v.扭曲；捻；扭伤；n.扭动；弯曲】: ▶Twist the lid to open the jar. (拧开罐子的盖子。) ▶He twisted his ankle. (他扭伤了脚踝。) ▶a twist in the road (道路的弯曲处)
scatter 【v.撒播；使散开；分散】: ▶The farmer scattered seeds in the field. (农民在地里播种。) ▶The crowd scattered when the police arrived. (警察到来时人群散开了。)
fold 【v.折叠；合拢；n.褶痕】: ▶Fold the letter and put it in the envelope. (把信折好放进信封。) ▶the folds of the curtain (窗帘的褶子)
fasten 【v.扣紧；系牢】: ▶Fasten your seatbelt. (系好安全带。)
loosen 【v.松开；放松】: ▶Loosen the screw a little. (把螺丝拧松一点。)
smash 【v.打碎；猛击；n.破碎声】: ▶He smashed the window with a stone. (他用石头打碎了窗户。) ▶the smash of breaking glass (玻璃破碎的声音)
scratch 【v.抓；搔；刮；n.抓痕；刮擦声】: ▶The cat scratched me. (猫抓了我。) ▶There's a scratch on the car door. (车门上有一道划痕。)
wipe 【v.&n.擦；揩】: ▶Wipe the table with a damp cloth. (用湿布擦桌子。) ▶Give the table a quick wipe. (把桌子快速擦一下。)
scrape 【v.刮掉；擦伤；n.刮擦声；擦伤】: ▶Scrape the mud off your shoes. (刮掉你鞋子上的泥。) ▶a scrape on the knee (膝盖上的擦伤)
polish 【v.擦亮；磨光；n.抛光剂；光泽】: ▶He polished his shoes until they shone. (他把鞋子擦得锃亮。) ▶shoe polish (鞋油)
peel 【v.剥皮；削皮；n.果皮】: ▶Peel the potatoes before boiling them. (煮土豆前先削皮。) ▶apple peel (苹果皮)
split 【v.分裂；撕裂；n.裂口；分歧】: ▶The wood split with a loud crack. (木头随着一声巨响裂开了。) ▶a split in the political party (政党内的分裂)
sway 【v.&n.摇摆；影响】: ▶The trees swayed in the wind. (树木在风中摇曳。) ▶His speech swayed many voters. (他的演讲影响了许多选民。)
shake 【v.摇动；颤抖；n.摇动；震动】: ▶Shake the bottle well before use. (使用前请充分摇晃瓶子。) ▶a shake of the head (摇头)
vibrate 【v.振动；颤动】: ▶The phone vibrated in his pocket. (手机在他口袋里振动。)
whirl 【v.&n.旋转；回旋】: ▶The leaves whirled in the wind. (树叶在风中旋转。) ▶My mind was in a whirl. (我的脑子一片混乱。)
rotate 【v.旋转；轮流】: ▶The Earth rotates on its axis. (地球绕地轴旋转。) ▶The crops are rotated each year. (庄稼每年轮作。)
reel 【v.卷；绕；蹒跚；n.卷轴】: ▶He reeled in the fishing line. (他卷收钓鱼线。) ▶He reeled from the shock. (他震惊得踉踉跄跄。) ▶a reel of film (一卷胶片)
shuffle 【v.拖着脚走；洗牌；乱堆】: ▶The old man shuffled across the room. (老人拖着脚走过房间。) ▶It's your turn to shuffle the cards. (轮到你洗牌了。)

wrap 【v.包；裹；n.披肩】: ▶She wrapped the gift in beautiful paper. (她用漂亮的纸把礼物包起来。)
penetrate 【v.穿透；渗透；洞察】: ▶The bullet penetrated the wall. (子弹穿透了墙壁。) ▶It's difficult to penetrate their secret organization. (很难打入他们的秘密组织。)
pierce 【v.刺穿；穿孔】: ▶The needle pierced her finger. (针扎破了她的手指。)

trail 【n.小径；踪迹；v.拖；追踪】: ▶a mountain trail (山间小径) ▶The dog trailed its master. (狗跟着主人走。)
arrange 【v.安排；整理；排列】: ▶I will arrange a meeting for next week. (我将安排下周开个会。) ▶She arranged the flowers in a vase. (她把花插在花瓶里。)
manipulate 【v.操纵；操作；巧妙地处理】: ▶He knows how to manipulate public opinion. (他知道如何操纵舆论。) ▶The pilot manipulates the controls of the aircraft. (飞行员操作飞机的控制器。)
steer 【v.驾驶；引导】: ▶He steered the boat into the harbour. (他把船开进港口。)
baptize 【v.给…施洗礼；命名】: ▶The baby was baptized in the church. (婴儿在教堂接受了洗礼。)
bet 【v.&n.打赌；赌博】: ▶I bet ten dollars on that horse. (我赌那匹马十美元。) ▶a safe bet (一个稳赢的赌注)
stake 【n.赌注；利害关系；v.以…打赌；资助】: ▶He has a stake in the company's success. (公司的成功与他利害攸关。) ▶I'd stake my reputation on it. (我敢拿我的名誉担保。)
gamble 【v.&n.赌博；冒险】: ▶It's dangerous to gamble with your health. (拿你的健康去冒险是危险的。) ▶Starting a business is always a gamble. (创业总是一场赌博。)

bewilder 【v.使迷惑；使糊涂】: ▶The complicated instructions bewildered me. (复杂的说明把我搞糊涂了。)

dispose 【v.处理；安排；使倾向于】: ▶How should we dispose of the waste? (我们该如何处理这些废物？) ▶I feel disposed to agree with you. (我倾向于同意你的意见。)
conduct 【v.组织；实施；引导；n.行为】: ▶They conducted a survey. (他们进行了一项调查。) ▶His conduct was unacceptable. (他的行为是不可接受的。)
omit 【v.省略；遗漏；忘记】: ▶She omitted an important detail from her report. (她在报告中遗漏了一个重要细节。)
delete 【v.删除】: ▶Delete the file from your computer. (从你的电脑上删除这个文件。)
cancel 【v.取消；撤销】: ▶The flight was cancelled due to bad weather. (航班因天气恶劣被取消。)
clear 【adj.清楚的；晴朗的；v.清除；使清楚】: ▶The instructions are very clear. (说明非常清楚。) ▶Please clear the table after dinner. (晚餐后请清理桌子。)
erase 【v.擦掉；清除】: ▶Erase the pencil marks. (擦掉铅笔痕迹。)
rescue 【v.&n.营救；救援】: ▶The firemen rescued the family from the burning building. (消防员从燃烧的大楼里救出了那家人。) ▶a rescue operation (救援行动)
resort 【n.度假胜地；手段；v.诉诸；求助】: ▶a ski resort (滑雪胜地) ▶as a last resort (作为最后的手段) ▶He resorted to violence. (他诉诸暴力。)
recover 【v.恢复；复原；重新获得】: ▶He is recovering from his illness. (他正在从疾病中恢复。) ▶The police recovered the stolen goods. (警方找回了被盗物品。)
restore 【v.恢复；修复；归还】: ▶They are trying to restore the old painting. (他们正在努力修复那幅古画。) ▶Order was quickly restored. (秩序很快恢复了。)
rectify 【v.纠正；矫正】: ▶We must rectify the mistake. (我们必须纠正这个错误。)
redeem 【v.弥补；赎回；拯救】: ▶He redeemed himself by apologizing. (他通过道歉弥补了自己的过错。)
offset 【v.抵消；补偿；n.补偿】: ▶The cost of the new furniture was offset by the savings on rent. (新家具的费用被节省下来的租金抵消了。)
replenish 【v.补充；重新装满】: ▶We need to replenish our supplies. (我们需要补充我们的物资。)
obtain 【v.获得；得到】: ▶You need to obtain a visa before you travel. (旅行前你需要获得签证。)
gain 【v.获得；增加；n.收益】: ▶She gained valuable experience from the job. (她从工作中获得了宝贵的经验。) ▶a gain in weight (体重增加)
supply 【v.供应；提供；n.供应品】: ▶The company supplies food to the restaurants. (该公司向餐馆供应食品。) ▶a supply of water (供水)
offer 【v.提供；提出；n.提议；报价】: ▶He offered me a job. (他给我提供了一份工作。) ▶a generous offer (慷慨的出价)
render 【v.使得；提供；翻译】: ▶His illness rendered him unable to work. (他的病使他无法工作。) ▶The jury rendered a verdict of guilty. (陪审团作出了有罪的裁决。)
enlarge 【v.扩大；放大】: ▶They plan to enlarge the house. (他们计划扩建房子。)
augment 【v.增加；扩大】: ▶He augmented his income by working overtime. (他通过加班来增加收入。)
magnify 【v.放大；扩大；夸大】: ▶This microscope magnifies objects 100 times. (这台显微镜能将物体放大100倍。)
amplify 【v.放大；增强；详述】: ▶We need to amplify the sound. (我们需要放大声音。)
exaggerate 【v.夸张；夸大】: ▶He tends to exaggerate his achievements. (他倾向于夸大自己的成就。)
prolong 【v.延长；拉长】: ▶The treatment may prolong his life. (治疗可能会延长他的生命。)
uphold 【v.支持；维护；维持】: ▶The court upheld the decision. (法院维持了原判。)
backup 【n.备份；后援；adj.备用的】: ▶Make a backup of your files. (给你的文件做个备份。) ▶a backup plan (备用计划)
propel 【v.推进；推动】: ▶The boat is propelled by a small motor. (这艘船由一台小马达推动。)
update 【v.更新；使现代化；n.更新】: ▶I need to update my software. (我需要更新我的软件。) ▶a news update (新闻更新)
raise 【v.举起；提高；筹集；抚养；n.加薪】: ▶Raise your hand if you know the answer. (如果你知道答案请举手。) ▶They are raising money for charity. (他们正在为慈善事业筹集资金。) ▶a pay raise (加薪)
leak 【v.漏；泄漏；n.漏洞；泄漏】: ▶The roof leaks when it rains. (下雨时屋顶漏水。) ▶a gas leak (煤气泄漏)
spill 【v.&n.溢出；洒出】: ▶I spilled coffee on my shirt. (我把咖啡洒在衬衫上了。) ▶an oil spill (石油泄漏)
seep 【v.渗出；漏】: ▶Water seeped through the cracks in the wall. (水从墙上的裂缝渗了进来。)
ooze 【v.渗出；分泌；n.软泥】: ▶Blood oozed from the cut. (血从伤口渗出来。)
evacuate 【v.疏散；撤离；排空】: ▶The building was evacuated because of the fire. (由于火灾，大楼里的人被疏散了。)
trench 【n.沟；战壕】: ▶The soldiers dug trenches for protection. (士兵们挖战壕以作掩护。)
saturate 【v.使饱和；浸透】: ▶The market is saturated with similar products. (市场上充斥着类似的产品。) ▶The rain saturated the ground. (雨水浸透了地面。)
excuse 【v.原谅；为…辩解；n.借口】: ▶Please excuse my late arrival. (请原谅我迟到了。) ▶a poor excuse (一个蹩脚的借口)
forgive 【v.原谅；宽恕】: ▶I forgive you for what you said. (我原谅你所说的话。)
contain 【v.包含；控制；遏制】: ▶The box contains old letters. (盒子里装着旧信件。) ▶Firefighters tried to contain the blaze. (消防员试图控制火势。)
regard 【v.认为；注视；n.尊重；问候】: ▶I regard him as a friend. (我把他当作朋友。) ▶Give my regards to your family. (代我向你的家人问好。)
flatter 【v.奉承；使高兴；衬托】: ▶He flattered her on her cooking. (他奉承她的厨艺。) ▶This photograph flatters you. (这张照片比你本人好看。)
worship 【v.&n.崇拜；敬奉】: ▶They worship God every Sunday. (他们每个星期天都敬拜上帝。) ▶the worship of money (拜金)
cause 【n.原因；事业；v.导致】: ▶The cause of the fire is unknown. (火灾的原因不明。) ▶a good cause (一项崇高的事业) ▶What caused the accident? (是什么导致了事故？)
sake 【n.缘故；理由】: ▶For the sake of your health, you should stop smoking. (为了你的健康，你应该戒烟。)
purpose 【n.目的；意图；用途】: ▶What is the purpose of your visit? (你访问的目的是什么？)
objective 【n.目标；目的；adj.客观的】: ▶Our main objective is to increase sales. (我们的主要目标是增加销售额。) ▶an objective opinion (一个客观的意见)
arouse 【v.引起；唤醒；激发】: ▶The noise aroused my curiosity. (这噪音引起了我的好奇心。)
trigger 【v.引发；触发；n.扳机】: ▶The incident triggered a chain of events. (该事件引发了一连串的事情。) ▶pull the trigger (扣动扳机)
seek 【v.寻找；寻求；探索】: ▶He is seeking a new job. (他正在寻找新工作。)
retrieve 【v.取回；找回；检索】: ▶I need to retrieve my file from the computer. (我需要从电脑里检索我的文件。)

enlighten 【v.启发；教导】: ▶Can you enlighten me on this subject? (你能在这个问题上启发我吗？)
impart 【v.传授；告知；赋予】: ▶A teacher imparts knowledge to students. (老师向学生传授知识。)
deserve 【v.应受；应得】: ▶She deserves a reward for her hard work. (她工作努力，应该得到奖励。)
drop 【v.落下；下降；放弃；n.滴；下降】: ▶The glass dropped from her hand. (玻璃杯从她手中掉落。) ▶a drop in temperature (温度下降)
sink 【v.下沉；沉没；n.水槽】: ▶The ship sank to the bottom of the ocean. (船沉到了海底。) ▶a kitchen sink (厨房水槽)
plummet 【v.垂直落下；暴跌】: ▶The plane plummeted towards the ground. (飞机垂直坠向地面。) ▶Stock prices plummeted. (股价暴跌。)
muffle 【v.压抑；消音；裹住】: ▶He muffled the sound with a pillow. (他用枕头捂住了声音。)

invite 【v.邀请；招致】: ▶They invited us to their wedding. (他们邀请我们参加他们的婚礼。) ▶His behavior invites criticism. (他的行为招致批评。)
welcome 【v.&n.欢迎；adj.受欢迎的】: ▶They welcomed us warmly. (他们热情地欢迎我们。) ▶a welcome guest (受欢迎的客人) ▶a warm welcome (热烈的欢迎)
greet 【v.问候；迎接；对…作出反应】: ▶He greeted me with a smile. (他微笑着向我打招呼。)

celebrate 【v.庆祝；颂扬】: ▶We celebrated his birthday with a party. (我们聚会庆祝他的生日。)

farewell 【n.&int.再见；告别；adj.告别的】: ▶a farewell party (告别聚会) ▶Farewell, my friend! (再见，我的朋友！)
assort 【v.把…分类；供应】: ▶assorted chocolates (什锦巧克力)
correspond 【v.符合；相当；通信】: ▶His actions do not correspond with his words. (他的言行不一。) ▶We correspond regularly. (我们定期通信。)
accord 【n.&v.一致；符合；授予】: ▶This is not in accord with the rules. (这与规则不符。) ▶He was accorded a hero's welcome. (他受到了英雄般的欢迎。)
attribute 【v.把…归因于；n.属性；特质】: ▶She attributes her success to hard work. (她将成功归因于努力工作。) ▶Patience is a good attribute for a teacher. (耐心是教师的一个良好品质。)
recall 【v.回忆起；召回；n.回忆；召回】: ▶I can't recall his name. (我想不起他的名字了。) ▶a product recall (产品召回)
recollect 【v.记起；回忆起】: ▶As far as I can recollect, she wasn't there. (据我回忆，她当时不在场。)

impress 【v.给…留下深刻印象；使铭记】: ▶Her speech impressed the audience. (她的演讲给观众留下了深刻印象。)
surmount 【v.克服；越过】: ▶She surmounted many obstacles to achieve her goal. (她克服了许多障碍来实现她的目标。)
mortify 【v.使羞辱；使难堪】: ▶He was mortified by his mistake. (他为自己的错误感到难堪。)
pervade 【v.弥漫；渗透；遍及】: ▶A sense of dread pervaded the city. (一种恐惧感弥漫了整个城市。)
replace 【v.代替；更换；放回原处】: ▶Can anything replace a mother's love? (有什么能代替母爱吗？) ▶Replace the books on the shelf. (把书放回书架。)
substitute 【n.代替者；代用品；v.代替】: ▶Tofu can be a substitute for meat. (豆腐可以代替肉类。) ▶She substituted for the sick teacher. (她代替生病的老师上课。)
distinguish 【v.区分；辨别；使杰出】: ▶It's hard to distinguish the twins. (很难区分这对双胞胎。) ▶He distinguished himself in the field of science. (他在科学领域表现杰出。)
differentiate 【v.区分；区别；使不同】: ▶Can you differentiate between these two species? (你能区分这两个物种吗？)
incline 【v.倾斜；倾向于；n.斜坡】: ▶The road inclines steeply. (这条路坡度很陡。) ▶I incline to agree with you. (我倾向于同意你的意见。) ▶a steep incline (一个陡坡)
lean 【v.倾斜；倚靠；adj.瘦的；贫乏的】: ▶The ladder leaned against the wall. (梯子靠在墙上。) ▶lean meat (瘦肉)
sideways 【adv.&adj.向侧面；侧身】: ▶He moved sideways through the narrow gap. (他侧身穿过狭窄的缝隙。) ▶a sideways glance (侧目一瞥)


feel 【v.感觉；触摸；认为；n.触觉；感觉】: ▶I feel happy today. (我今天感到很开心。) ▶The silk feels smooth. (丝绸摸起来很光滑。) ▶I feel that it is a good idea. (我认为这是个好主意。) ▶The room has a warm feel to it. (这个房间给人一种温暖的感觉。)
mood 【n.心情；情绪；气氛】: ▶She is in a good mood today. (她今天心情很好。)
emotion 【n.情感；情绪；激动】: ▶He showed no emotion during the trial. (他在审判过程中没有表露任何情感。)

manner 【n.方式；举止；礼貌】: ▶She answered in a polite manner. (她礼貌地回答了问题。) ▶It's bad manners to interrupt. (打断别人是不礼貌的。)
attitude 【n.态度；看法；姿势】: ▶He has a positive attitude towards work. (他对工作持积极态度。)
character 【n.性格；特性；角色；字符】: ▶She is a woman of strong character. (她是个性格坚强的女人。) ▶The main character in the novel is a detective. (小说的主角是一名侦探。)
personality 【n.个性；人格；名人】: ▶He has a cheerful personality. (他性格开朗。)
trait 【n.特点；特性】: ▶Honesty is a desirable trait. (诚实是一个可贵的品质。)
virtue 【n.美德；优点】: ▶Patience is a virtue. (耐心是一种美德。)
feature 【n.特征；特色；v.以…为特色；主演】: ▶The island's main feature is its beautiful beach. (这个岛的主要特色是它美丽的海滩。) ▶The film features a famous actor. (这部电影由一位著名演员主演。)
stature 【n.身高；地位】: ▶He was a man of short stature but great influence. (他身材矮小，但影响力巨大。)
flesh 【n.肉；肉体；果肉】: ▶The trap cut into the animal's flesh. (陷阱割伤了动物的肉。) ▶the flesh of the peach (桃子的果肉)
mankind 【n.人类】: ▶a great contribution to mankind (对人类的巨大贡献)
human 【n.人；人类；adj.人的；人性的】: ▶Humans are social animals. (人是社会性动物。) ▶the human body (人体)
bone 【n.骨；骨头】: ▶He broke a bone in his arm. (他手臂骨折了。)

mind 【n.头脑；精神；v.介意；照顾】: ▶Her mind was full of questions. (她满脑子都是问题。) ▶Would you mind closing the window? (你介意关下窗吗？)

tongue 【n.舌头；语言】: ▶The doctor asked me to stick out my tongue. (医生让我伸出舌头。) ▶his native tongue (他的母语)

limb 【n.肢；臂；腿；树枝】: ▶He lost a limb in the accident. (他在事故中失去了一条肢体。) ▶a limb of a tree (树枝)
elbow 【n.肘；肘部；v.用肘推】: ▶She sat with her elbows on the table. (她坐着，胳膊肘支在桌子上。) ▶He elbowed his way through the crowd. (他用肘推挤着穿过人群。)

prescription 【n.处方；药方；开处方】: ▶The doctor wrote me a prescription. (医生给我开了一张处方。)

X-ray 【n.X射线；X光照片；v.用X光检查】: ▶The doctor took an X-ray of my chest. (医生给我的胸部拍了X光片。) ▶They X-rayed my leg. (他们用X光检查了我的腿。)
injection 【n.注射；注入】: ▶The nurse gave me an injection. (护士给我打了一针。)

grief 【n.悲痛；悲伤】: ▶She was overcome with grief. (她悲痛欲绝。)
grieve 【v.感到悲痛；使伤心】: ▶She grieved for her dead husband. (她为死去的丈夫感到悲痛。)
miserable 【adj.痛苦的；悲惨的；令人难受的】: ▶a miserable life (悲惨的生活) ▶miserable weather (令人难受的天气)
distress 【n.悲痛；危难；v.使悲痛；使忧虑】: ▶a ship in distress (遇险的船只) ▶The news distressed her greatly. (这个消息使她非常悲痛。)
sadness 【n.悲哀；悲伤】: ▶There was a deep sadness in her eyes. (她眼里流露出深深的悲伤。)
gloomy 【adj.阴暗的；沮丧的；悲观的】: ▶a gloomy day (阴暗的一天) ▶a gloomy mood (沮丧的心情)
disappoint 【v.使失望】: ▶The movie disappointed me. (这部电影让我失望。)
discourage 【v.使气馁；阻止】: ▶Don't let one failure discourage you. (不要因为一次失败就气馁。)
wretched 【adj.可怜的；悲惨的；恶劣的】: ▶the wretched poor (可怜的穷人) ▶wretched weather (恶劣的天气)
frustrating 【adj.令人沮丧的；令人挫败的】: ▶a frustrating experience (一次令人沮丧的经历)
mourn 【v.哀悼；忧伤】: ▶They mourned the loss of their leader. (他们哀悼领袖的逝世。)
anger 【n.愤怒；怒气；v.激怒】: ▶He could not control his anger. (他无法控制自己的愤怒。) ▶Her words angered him. (她的话激怒了他。)
furious 【adj.狂怒的；激烈的】: ▶She was furious with him. (她对他大发雷霆。) ▶a furious argument (激烈的争论)
frown 【v.&n.皱眉；蹙额】: ▶She frowned when she saw the mess. (看到混乱的场面，她皱起了眉头。) ▶a deep frown (深深的皱眉)
rage 【n.盛怒；狂暴；v.发怒；肆虐】: ▶He was trembling with rage. (他气得发抖。) ▶The fire raged for hours. (大火肆虐了数小时。)
irritate 【v.激怒；使烦躁；使不适】: ▶His constant whistling irritates me. (他不停的口哨声让我烦躁。) ▶The smoke irritated my eyes. (烟熏得我眼睛不舒服。)
hate 【v.憎恨；厌恶；n.憎恨；厌恶】: ▶I hate violence. (我憎恨暴力。) ▶She looked at him with hate. (她用憎恨的目光看着他。)
hatred 【n.憎恨；仇恨】: ▶racial hatred (种族仇恨)
nuisance 【n.讨厌的人或东西；麻烦事】: ▶Flies are a nuisance. (苍蝇是讨厌的东西。)
disgust 【n.厌恶；憎恶；v.使厌恶】: ▶She walked away in disgust. (她厌恶地走开了。) ▶The smell disgusted me. (这气味让我恶心。)
vex 【v.使烦恼；使苦恼】: ▶This problem has vexed me for weeks. (这个问题困扰了我好几个星期。)
harass 【v.骚扰；烦扰】: ▶She was harassed by phone calls. (她受到电话骚扰。)
bore 【v.使厌烦；钻；n.令人讨厌的人或事】: ▶His long speech bored the audience. (他的长篇大论让听众感到厌烦。) ▶He bored a hole in the wood. (他在木头上钻了一个洞。) ▶He is such a bore. (他真是个讨厌鬼。)
bother 【v.打扰；烦扰；n.麻烦；烦恼】: ▶I'm sorry to bother you. (抱歉打扰你。) ▶It's no bother. (这不麻烦。)
troublesome 【adj.麻烦的；令人烦恼的】: ▶a troublesome child (一个令人烦恼的孩子)
awful 【adj.糟糕的；可怕的；非常的】: ▶awful weather (糟糕的天气) ▶an awful lot of money (非常多的钱)
unpleasant 【adj.令人不快的；讨厌的】: ▶an unpleasant smell (难闻的气味)
adverse 【adj.不利的；有害的；相反的】: ▶adverse weather conditions (不利的天气条件) ▶an adverse reaction (不良反应)
hostile 【adj.敌对的；不友善的】: ▶a hostile crowd (敌对的人群) ▶a hostile environment (不友善的环境)
indignant 【adj.愤慨的；义愤的】: ▶She was indignant at the unfair treatment. (她对不公平的待遇感到愤慨。)
radical 【adj.根本的；激进的；n.激进分子】: ▶a radical change (根本性的改变) ▶a radical politician (一个激进的政治家)
mad 【adj.疯的；愚蠢的；狂热的】: ▶He went mad after the tragedy. (悲剧发生后他疯了。) ▶a mad idea (一个愚蠢的想法) ▶He is mad about football. (他对足球很狂热。)
crazy 【adj.疯狂的；荒唐的；狂热的】: ▶a crazy plan (一个疯狂的计划) ▶She is crazy about him. (她为他疯狂。)
wicked 【adj.邪恶的；缺德的；淘气的】: ▶a wicked witch (邪恶的女巫) ▶a wicked sense of humour (恶作剧的幽默感)
vicious 【adj.恶毒的；凶残的；剧烈的】: ▶a vicious attack (恶毒的攻击) ▶a vicious circle (恶性循环)
vulgar 【adj.粗俗的；庸俗的】: ▶vulgar language (粗俗的语言)
mean 【adj.卑鄙的；吝啬的；平均的；v.意思是；打算；n.平均值】: ▶a mean trick (卑鄙的伎俩) ▶He is very mean with his money. (他对钱很吝啬。) ▶the mean temperature (平均温度) ▶What does this word mean? (这个词是什么意思？) ▶I didn't mean to hurt you. (我不是故意要伤害你。)
ego 【n.自我；自尊】: ▶a blow to his ego (对他自尊的打击)
selfish 【adj.自私的；利己的】: ▶a selfish person (一个自私的人)
nasty 【adj.恶毒的；令人不快的；严重的】: ▶a nasty smell (难闻的气味) ▶a nasty accident (严重的事故)
rash 【adj.轻率的；鲁莽的；n.皮疹】: ▶a rash decision (一个轻率的决定) ▶a skin rash (皮疹)
volatile 【adj.易变的；不稳定的；易挥发的】: ▶a volatile situation (不稳定的局势) ▶a volatile liquid (易挥发的液体)
weird 【adj.怪异的；不可思议的】: ▶a weird dream (一个怪异的梦)
excessive 【adj.过分的；过多的】: ▶excessive drinking (过量饮酒)
anxiety 【n.焦虑；挂念；渴望】: ▶anxiety about the future (对未来的焦虑)
restless 【adj.焦躁不安的；静不下来的】: ▶a restless child (一个静不下来的孩子)
uneasy 【adj.心神不安的；不稳定的】: ▶I feel uneasy about the situation. (我对局势感到不安。)
fear 【n.害怕；恐惧；v.害怕；担心】: ▶a fear of heights (恐高症) ▶I fear that I may be late. (我担心我可能会迟到。)
timid 【adj.胆小的；羞怯的】: ▶a timid animal (胆小的动物)
fuss 【n.忙乱；大惊小怪；v.忙乱；过分关心】: ▶What's all the fuss about? (为什么这么大惊小怪？) ▶She fussed over her children. (她过分关心她的孩子们。)
insult 【v.&n.侮辱；辱骂】: ▶He insulted her intelligence. (他侮辱了她的智商。) ▶a terrible insult (严重的侮辱)
unkind 【adj.不友善的；刻薄的】: ▶an unkind remark (刻薄的话)
envy 【n.&v.羡慕；嫉妒】: ▶He looked with envy at her new car. (他羡慕地看着她的新车。) ▶I envy your happiness. (我羡慕你的幸福。)
jealous 【adj.妒忌的；猜疑的；珍惜的】: ▶a jealous husband (一个善妒的丈夫) ▶He is jealous of his reputation. (他很珍惜自己的名誉。)
doubt 【n.怀疑；疑问；v.怀疑；不信】: ▶I have my doubts about his story. (我对他的说法有怀疑。) ▶I doubt whether he will come. (我怀疑他是否会来。)
suspicion 【n.怀疑；疑心】: ▶He was arrested on suspicion of murder. (他因涉嫌谋杀而被捕。)
sceptical 【adj.怀疑的；怀疑论的】: ▶I am sceptical about his promises. (我对他的承诺表示怀疑。)
unsatisfactory 【adj.不能令人满意的】: ▶an unsatisfactory answer (一个不能令人满意的回答)
unstable 【adj.不稳定的；易变的】: ▶an unstable government (不稳定的政府)
unsuitable 【adj.不合适的；不适宜的】: ▶clothes unsuitable for cold weather (不适合寒冷天气的衣服)
unwilling 【adj.不愿意的；不情愿的】: ▶He was unwilling to help. (他不愿意帮忙。)
reluctant 【adj.不情愿的；勉强的】: ▶a reluctant participant (一个不情愿的参与者)
hesitate 【v.犹豫；踌躇】: ▶Don't hesitate to ask for help. (不要犹豫，尽管求助。)
confuse 【v.使困惑；混淆】: ▶The instructions confused me. (这些说明让我困惑。) ▶Don't confuse Austria with Australia. (别把奥地利和澳大利亚搞混了。)
guilty 【adj.有罪的；内疚的】: ▶The jury found him guilty. (陪审团裁定他有罪。) ▶I feel guilty about forgetting her birthday. (我为忘了她的生日而感到内疚。)
embarrass 【v.使窘迫；使尴尬】: ▶His question embarrassed her. (他的问题让她很尴尬。)
regret 【v.&n.后悔；遗憾；惋惜】: ▶I regret what I said. (我后悔我说的话。) ▶Much to my regret, I cannot accept your invitation. (非常遗憾，我不能接受你的邀请。)
repent 【v.悔悟；后悔】: ▶He repented of his sins. (他悔悟了自己的罪过。)
ashamed 【adj.惭愧的；羞耻的】: ▶You should be ashamed of yourself. (你应该为自己感到羞愧。)
sigh 【v.&n.叹气；叹息】: ▶She sighed with relief. (她宽慰地叹了口气。) ▶a deep sigh (一声深深的叹息)
weep 【v.哭泣；流泪】: ▶She wept for joy. (她喜极而泣。)
tolerance 【n.宽容；容忍；忍耐力】: ▶religious tolerance (宗教宽容)
ignorant 【adj.无知的；愚昧的】: ▶He is ignorant of the facts. (他对事实一无所知。)
endure 【v.忍受；容忍；持续】: ▶She endured years of pain. (她忍受了多年的痛苦。) ▶His fame will endure forever. (他的名声将永存。)
sly 【adj.狡猾的；狡诈的】: ▶a sly fox (狡猾的狐狸)
cunning 【adj.&n.狡猾的；狡诈的】: ▶a cunning plan (一个狡猾的计划) ▶He showed great cunning. (他表现得非常狡猾。)
arbitrary 【adj.任意的；武断的；专制的】: ▶an arbitrary decision (一个武断的决定)
ridiculous 【adj.可笑的；荒谬的】: ▶a ridiculous idea (一个荒谬的想法)
stupid 【adj.愚蠢的；迟钝的】: ▶a stupid mistake (一个愚蠢的错误)
awkward 【adj.笨拙的；尴尬的；难处理的】: ▶an awkward movement (笨拙的动作) ▶an awkward silence (尴尬的沉默) ▶an awkward shape (难处理的形状)
clumsy 【adj.笨拙的；不得体的】: ▶clumsy fingers (笨拙的手指) ▶a clumsy apology (不得体的道歉)
careless 【adj.粗心的；疏忽的】: ▶a careless driver (粗心的司机)
oblivious 【adj.未察觉的；不注意的】: ▶He was oblivious to the danger. (他没有察觉到危险。)
naughty 【adj.顽皮的；淘气的】: ▶a naughty child (一个顽皮的孩子)
greedy 【adj.贪婪的；贪吃的】: ▶a greedy man (一个贪婪的人)
obtrusive 【adj.冒失的；显眼的】: ▶obtrusive behavior (冒失的行为) ▶an obtrusive building (一栋显眼的建筑)
slothful 【adj.懒惰的】: ▶a slothful person (一个懒惰的人)
sluggish 【adj.行动迟缓的；缺乏活力的】: ▶a sluggish economy (缺乏活力的经济)
impulse 【n.冲动；推动力；脉冲】: ▶He bought the car on impulse. (他一时冲动买了那辆车。)
rigid 【adj.僵硬的；死板的；严格的】: ▶a rigid structure ( rigid 的结构) ▶rigid rules (死板的规定)
stubborn 【adj.顽固的；执拗的】: ▶a stubborn child (一个固执的孩子)
stereotype 【n.陈规；老套；v.对…形成刻板印象】: ▶racial stereotypes (种族刻板印象) ▶It's wrong to stereotype people. (对人形成刻板印象是不对的。)


daily 【adj.每日的；日常的；adv.每日；n.日报】: ▶He takes a daily walk in the park. (他每天在公园散步。) ▶The milk is delivered daily. (牛奶每日送达。) ▶I read the news in the daily. (我在日报上看新闻。)
monthly 【adj.每月的；adv.每月；n.月刊】: ▶We have a monthly meeting. (我们每月开一次会。) ▶The magazine is published monthly. (这本杂志每月出版一期。) ▶a women's monthly (一本女性月刊)
quarterly 【adj.&adv.季度的；n.季刊】: ▶a quarterly report (季度报告) ▶The interest is paid quarterly. (利息按季度支付。) ▶a literary quarterly (文学季刊)
annual 【adj.每年的；年度的；n.年鉴；一年生植物】: ▶The company holds an annual party. (公司每年举行一次聚会。) ▶I bought an annual for gardening. (我买了一本园艺年鉴。)
yearly 【adj.&adv.每年的；一年一度的】: ▶a yearly check-up (年度体检) ▶We visit them yearly. (我们每年拜访他们一次。)
anniversary 【n.周年纪念日】: ▶They celebrated their wedding anniversary. (他们庆祝了结婚纪念日。)
era 【n.时代；纪元】: ▶the Victorian era (维多利亚时代)
present 【adj.现在的；出席的；n.礼物；现在；v.呈现；介绍】: ▶the present situation (当前形势) ▶All the members were present. (所有成员都出席了。) ▶a birthday present (生日礼物) ▶the past, present and future (过去、现在和未来) ▶She presented her findings to the committee. (她向委员会陈述了她的发现。)
contemporary 【adj.当代的；同时代的；n.同代人；当代人】: ▶contemporary art (当代艺术) ▶Shakespeare and his contemporaries (莎士比亚和他的同代人)
medieval 【adj.中世纪的】: ▶a medieval castle (一座中世纪城堡)

billion 【n.十亿；adj.十亿的】: ▶The government spent billions on the project. (政府在这个项目上花费了数十亿。) ▶a billion stars (十亿颗星星)
dozen 【n.十二个；一打】: ▶I bought a dozen eggs. (我买了一打鸡蛋。)
dawn 【n.黎明；开端；v.破晓；开始出现】: ▶We left at dawn. (我们黎明时分出发。) ▶the dawn of civilization (文明的开端) ▶A new day dawned. (新的一天开始了。)
midday 【n.正午；中午】: ▶We will meet at midday. (我们将在正午见面。)
midnight 【n.午夜；子夜】: ▶The party went on until midnight. (聚会持续到午夜。)
overnight 【adv.在晚上；突然；adj.夜间的；突然的】: ▶We stayed overnight in a hotel. (我们在酒店住了一晚。) ▶an overnight success (一夜成名) ▶an overnight bag (过夜包)
night 【n.夜；夜晚】: ▶I slept well last night. (我昨晚睡得很好。)
modern 【adj.现代的；现代化的】: ▶modern technology (现代科技)
recent 【adj.最近的；近来的】: ▶recent events (最近的事件)
up-to-date 【adj.最新的；现代的】: ▶up-to-date information (最新信息)
first 【adj.第一的；最初的；adv.首先；第一次；n.第一】: ▶the first chapter (第一章) ▶First, I would like to thank you all. (首先，我想感谢大家。) ▶She was the first to arrive. (她是第一个到的。)
secondly 【adv.第二；其次】: ▶Firstly, it's expensive; secondly, it's unnecessary. (首先，它很贵；其次，它没必要。)
finally 【adv.最后；终于】: ▶Finally, I would like to say... (最后，我想说……) ▶He finally agreed. (他终于同意了。)
finish 【v.完成；结束；n.结束；终点】: ▶Have you finished your homework? (你做完作业了吗？) ▶the finish of the race (赛跑的终点)
immediately 【adv.立即；马上；conj.一…就…】: ▶Please come here immediately. (请马上到这里来。) ▶I recognized her immediately I saw her. (我一见到她就认出了她。)
instant 【adj.立即的；即食的；n.瞬间；片刻】: ▶an instant success (一举成功) ▶instant coffee (速溶咖啡) ▶It all happened in an instant. (一切发生在一瞬间。)
moment 【n.片刻；瞬间；时机】: ▶Wait a moment, please. (请稍等片刻。) ▶a moment of silence (默哀时刻)
minute 【n.分钟；片刻；adj.微小的；详细的】: ▶The meeting will start in ten minutes. (会议将在十分钟后开始。) ▶minute details (微小的细节)
prior 【adj.在先的；优先的】: ▶I have a prior engagement. (我有约在先。)
former 【adj.以前的；前者的；n.前者】: ▶her former husband (她的前夫) ▶Of the two options, I prefer the former. (在这两个选项中，我更喜欢前者。)
preceding 【adj.在前的；前面的】: ▶the preceding chapter (前一章)
precedent 【n.先例；范例】: ▶This decision sets a precedent. (这个决定开创了一个先例。)
foremost 【adj.最重要的；第一流的；adv.首先】: ▶He is one of the foremost scientists in his field. (他是他所在领域最重要的科学家之一。) ▶First and foremost, we must ensure safety. (首先，我们必须确保安全。)
opening 【n.开始；开口；空缺；adj.开始的；开幕的】: ▶the opening of the ceremony (典礼的开始) ▶an opening in the wall (墙上的一个洞) ▶an opening speech (开幕词)
initially 【adv.最初；开头】: ▶Initially, I disagreed with the plan. (起初，我不同意这个计划。)
intermediate 【adj.中间的；中级的】: ▶an intermediate level (中级水平)
midst 【n.中间；中部】: ▶in the midst of the crowd (在人群中间)
meantime 【n.其间；同时】: ▶The next program will start soon; in the meantime, here's some music. (下一个节目马上开始；在此期间，请听一些音乐。)
meanwhile 【adv.与此同时；在此期间】: ▶I was cooking dinner. Meanwhile, my husband was setting the table. (我在做晚饭，与此同时，我丈夫在摆餐具。)
simultaneous 【adj.同时的；同步的】: ▶There were simultaneous explosions in two cities. (两个城市同时发生了爆炸。)
ongoing 【adj.持续存在的；进行中的】: ▶an ongoing debate (持续的辩论)
everlasting 【adj.永久的；永恒的】: ▶everlasting love (永恒的爱)
permanent 【adj.永久的；持久的】: ▶a permanent address (永久地址)
punctual 【adj.准时的；守时的】: ▶Please be punctual for the meeting. (请准时参加会议。)
duration 【n.持续期间】: ▶the duration of the war (战争期间)
consecutive 【adj.连续的；连贯的】: ▶It rained for three consecutive days. (连续下了三天雨。)
periodically 【adv.周期性地；定期地】: ▶The machine should be checked periodically. (这台机器应该定期检查。)
imminent 【adj.即将发生的；迫近的】: ▶A storm is imminent. (暴风雨即将来临。)
incidentally 【adv.顺便提一句；附带地】: ▶Incidentally, have you seen my keys? (顺便问一句，你看到我的钥匙了吗？)
